# PLAN SKETCHER SUITE — SESSION HANDOFF
*Updated: 2026-06-24 (rev 60 — **SEISMIC — 2-STORY MODULE: per-diaphragm weight + vertical force distribution. 2-STORY SEISMIC NOW WORKING (uniform + mixed-height C/D).** (1) **Per-level seismic weight.** New pure `seismicWeight2Story(graph, loop, twoStoryLoop, propsFor, isOne, roofDL, floorDL, wallDL)` splits the tributary WALL weight between the two diaphragms per SECTION-B: roof (Level 2) wall trib = `par + H₂/2` (full parapet + upper half of story 2) summed over the **2-story walls only**; floor (Level 1) wall trib = `H₂/2 + H₁/2` for a 2-story wall, `par + H₁/2` for a **1-story-tagged** wall (mixed-height C/D — a 1-story wall reaches the floor diaphragm but not the roof). Area DL by level: the 2-story footprint (`twoStoryLoop.area`) carries floorDL at L1 + roofDL at L2; any 1-story-only footprint carries roofDL at L1. Diaphragm elevations `h_floor = H₁`, `h_roof = H₁ + H₂`. (2) **Vertical distribution (Phase 3).** New `seismicDistribute2Story(sw2, Cs)` → `V = Cs·W_total`, then `F_level = V·(W_level·h_level)/Σ(W·h)` → `F_roof`, `F_floor`. (3) **Per-level plan plf (Phase 4) + floor-aware draw.** The seismic distribution now uses the ACTIVE-floor force: roof view (Level 2) distributes `F_roof` on the **2-story-only walls** (`twoStoryGraph`/`twoStoryLoop` — the roof diaphragm exists only there); floor view (Level 1) distributes `F_floor` on the full graph. `w = F_level / (bounding-box extent ⟂ the force)`, computed from the diaphragm's own bbox (so a mixed building's roof spreads over the 2-story footprint). Reuses the rev-58 generalized `buildSecData` `{base:()=>w, lee:()=>0}` + the guarded `lineReactions` — so the per-level base shear is conserved and wall reactions are produced exactly like wind/1-story. The Plan/Design floor selector switches between the roof + floor seismic loads automatically. (4) **Display.** The 2-Story Seismic Weight card (was a "coming later" placeholder) now shows per-level W (area + wall split), W_total, V, the story forces F_roof/F_floor, and the per-level plan plf for the selected floor; `wTotal` lifted to App also covers 2-story now (Design Seismic card shows `V = Cs·W` in 2-story too). **Guard:** `calcCore.js` + all 8 must-hold app-file guarded fns BYTE-IDENTICAL; `buildSecData` unchanged since rev 58 (the new helpers are pure, outside the engine). VIEW-ONLY (seismic reactions still don't drive the Design-tab demand). Verified: compile CLEAN; engine guard CLEAN; **Phase-5 test case EXACT** — W_roof 86,004 / W_floor 157,986 / W_total 243,990; V 12,199.5; F_roof 5,985.2 / F_floor 6,214.3 lbs (spec's 5,984.8/6,214.7 are hand-rounding artifacts of an intermediate ratio); plan plf land on **153.46/99.75 (roof) + 159.35/103.58 (floor)** as expected; end-to-end pipeline conserves each level's force through `buildSecData`+reactions (14/14); mixed-height C/D routing 5/5 (a 1-story wall → 0 roof trib, `par+H₁/2` floor trib); SSR mount PASS wind (36,899) + 2-story-seismic (43,951). `APP_BUILD = 139` ("Version 1.39"). Prior rev — rev 59 — **SEISMIC, STEP 3 of 3 — base-shear distribution to plan boundary (plf) + reactions + Wind/Seismic view toggle; Cs input moved to the Plan tab (user-requested). 1-STORY SEISMIC MODULE NOW COMPLETE.** (1) **Cs relocated.** The `Cs` input moved from the Design tab to the Plan-tab **Dead Loads** card (with Roof/Floor/Wall DL); the Design "Seismic" card now shows `Cs` + `V` READ-ONLY. (2) **Seismic distribution.** `V = Cs·W_total` is spread as a uniform line load `w = V / projected-extent` along the boundary faces perpendicular to each direction — force X (axis "h") → `w = V/Dy` on the Y-running faces, force Y (axis "v") → `w = V/Dx` on the X-running faces (`Dx`/`Dy` = plan bounding-box extents). Implemented by calling the rev-58 generalized `buildSecData` with a uniform load model `{ base:()=>w, lee:()=>0 }` per direction (`secSeisH`/`secSeisV`), so the existing windward-collection + across-wind shadow + **guarded `lineReactions`** geometry distributes V (conserving it) and produces the wall point-load reactions — no new reaction code. (3) **Plan visualization + toggle.** A new **Load case** segmented toggle (**Wind | Seismic**) in the top ribbon; in Seismic view the canvas draws BOTH directions' plf line loads (`WindLoad`, gained a `prec` prop → seismic labels show 2 decimals) and their reactions (`Reaction`) instead of the wind section loads — `dispH`/`dispV` switch on `loadCase`. Seismic loads aren't section-cut-editable (no `onOpen`). The Seismic Weight card shows V and the per-direction face plf; `loadCase` persists in the session (additive). **VIEW-ONLY for now** — the seismic reactions are shown but do NOT yet drive the Design-tab seismic demand (still the manual `g.vSeismic`); 1-story only (2-Story shows "—"/pending). **Guard:** `calcCore.js` + all 7 must-hold guarded fns BYTE-IDENTICAL; `buildSecData` unchanged since rev 58 (Option B) — wind output re-confirmed byte-identical by `work/_golden.cjs`. `WindLoad`/`Reaction` are presentational (not guarded). Prior rev — rev 58 — **SEISMIC, STEP 2 of 3 — base shear V + the Option-B engine generalization; ALL dead-load inputs now on the Plan tab (user-requested).** (1) **Entire Loads box removed from the Design tab.** Per the user, the whole "Loads" `PinCard` is gone from the Design tab; **Floor DL** joined Roof DL + Wall DL in the Plan-tab **Dead Loads** card (all three psf inputs now live on the Plan tab — 2-story seismic will use Floor DL). The values stay in the shared `g` (`g.roofDL`/`g.floorDL`/`g.wallDL`), so the Design/Calc uplift formula in `calcCore.js` (`wdl = roofTrib·roofDL + floorTrib·floorDL + wallDL·h`) reads them **exactly as before** — relocation only, no calc change. (2) **`Cs` + `V`.** New `g.Cs` (Seismic Response Coefficient, default 0.05); a new **Seismic** `PinCard` on the Design tab holds the `Cs` input and shows `V = Cs·W_total`; the Plan-tab Seismic Weight card also shows the `V` row. `W_total` is lifted from `PlanSketcher` to `App` (`wTotal`, null in 2-Story → "—") via a one-line effect so both tabs can display `V`. (3) **Option B — `buildSecData` generalized.** Its per-wall line load now comes from a `loadModel` parameter; the DEFAULT `WIND_LOAD` model reproduces the exact wind arithmetic verbatim (`base = ½·H·pw + par·qWind`, `lee = leePar·qLee`), so the wind path is unchanged, and a seismic caller (Step 3) will pass `{ base:()=>V/extent, lee:()=>0 }`. **This is the one guarded-engine change** (user-approved). **Guard:** `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; the other 7 app-file guarded fns (incl. `lineReactions`) BYTE-IDENTICAL; `buildSecData` intentionally changed and its **wind output proven byte-identical** by a golden-output regression (`work/_golden.cjs`) over a rectangle + an L-shape in all 4 directions. Prior rev — rev 57 — **SEISMIC, STEP 1 of 3 — effective seismic weight (W_total), 1-story (user-requested).** First step of the seismic module. (1) **Dead-load inputs relocated:** the Roof DL and Wall DL (psf) inputs moved from the Design-tab "Loads" card to the **Plan Sketcher** side panel (new **Dead Loads** card), because they drive the building's seismic weight — a geometry-phase quantity. The values still live in the shared `g` (`g.roofDL` / `g.wallDL`), so the uplift dead-load formula in `calcCore.js` (`wdl = roofTrib·roofDL + floorTrib·floorDL + wallDL·h`) reads them unchanged; Floor DL stays on the Design tab. `g`/`setGl` are now threaded into `PlanSketcher`. (2) **New pure helper `seismicWeight1Story(graph, loop, propsFor, roofDL, wallDL)`:** `W_roof = enclosed area × roofDL`; per wall `H_trib = par + H/2` (full parapet above the diaphragm + half the story below, the lower half spanning to the foundation), `W = H_trib × length × wallDL`, summed to `W_wall`; `W_total = W_roof + W_wall`. Reads each wall's own `par`/`H` (so it tracks Global Inputs / section cuts) and returns a per-parapet-profile breakdown. **1-STORY ONLY** — in 2-Story mode the Seismic Weight card shows a "coming in a later step" note (the per-diaphragm tributary split lands with the 2-story schematics). (3) **Display:** a new **Seismic Weight** card on the Plan side panel shows roof area, W_roof, W_wall, W_total (lbs), and the by-profile breakdown. **NO engine change:** `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; all 8 app-file guarded fns byte-identical (this step adds a pure helper + UI only). Verified: esbuild bundle-compile CLEAN; engine byte-identity CLEAN; **Phase-4 unit test PASS — W_total = 88,542 lbs** on the 60×39 / roofDL 20 / wallDL 18 / H 13 / par 6&4 case (profiles 27,000 + 14,742; roof 46,800). `APP_BUILD = 136` ("Version 1.36"). Prior rev — rev 56 — **GLOBAL INPUTS — set wall height, parapet height, and wind pressures for the WHOLE building at once (user-requested).** A new **Global Inputs** button in the Plan Sketcher side panel (a card just below Live Metrics) opens a window that writes wall + parapet parameters to EVERY wall in one action, so a building with uniform walls no longer needs a section cut per wall. The fields map onto the EXISTING per-wall props — **no new data-model field, no `.wps` schema change.** 1-Story mode fields: Wall Height→`H` · Parapet Height→`par` · Wall Pressure→`pw` · Windward / Leeward Parapet Pressure→`qWind` / `qLee` (all applied to every wall). 2-Story mode: 1st / 2nd Level Wall Height→`H` / `H2` (all walls); the three pressures are NOT split by level → `pw` / `qWind` / `qLee` (all walls); and the two parapet HEIGHTS route by level — **1st Level Parapet Height → `par` on walls tagged 1-story**, **2nd Level Parapet Height → `par` on the full-height 2-story walls** (each physical wall still carries exactly ONE `par`, so this routes the existing field, it does not add a `par2`). New `GlobalInputsWindow` component, modeled on `DLTributaryWindow` (`.ovl`/`.win` chrome, per-field string buffers, an explicit **Apply to all walls** button rather than live-per-keystroke, since it is a building-wide action). Opening seeds each field from the building-wide CONSENSUS (uniform → that value; mixed or empty → the `DEF_SECTION` default; `par1`/`par2` seed from the 1-story / 2-story walls respectively). `applyGlobalInputs` writes `wallProps` for all edges in ONE `setWallProps`, spreading the current entry first so per-wall DL tributary (and any other field) survives; 1-Story mode leaves `H2` untouched. Everything downstream (on-plan loads/reactions, section cuts, design handoff, the rev-51/52 stale-push signatures) is already reactive to `wallProps`, so there is **NO engine touch** — and a global apply correctly re-arms the Design-tab stale indicators because the handoff signature changes. **`calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; all 8 app-file guarded fns byte-identical.** Verified: esbuild bundle-compile CLEAN (modular app AND the single-file preview bundle); `calcCore.js` + the 8 guarded fns diffed byte-identical vs the upload. Per the user's request this session the full SSR / logic harness was NOT run — verification was compile + engine byte-identity only. `APP_BUILD = 135` ("Version 1.35"). Prior rev — rev 53 — **CALCULATION SHEET IS NOW A CHROME-STYLE SUB-TAB SURFACE + WALL-NAME CONSISTENCY ACROSS TABS (user-requested).** Three coordinated changes spanning the Design and Calculation tabs. (1) **Design line naming** — each design line's chip/title now carries an incrementing per-direction index: "E–W-1", "E–W-2", "N–S-1", … (new `lineNames` memo in `DesignTab`, counting within each `windAxis`; `lineLabel(ln)` = name + force + length). Positional like the `SW-A` marks (tracks a line's position in the floor's list, not a persisted id). (2) **Calc sub-tabs** — the Calculation Sheet is now a tabbed surface (one pinned, Chrome-style sub-tab per shear-wall line). App state moved from a single `segments`/`g.wWind` to `calcTabs = [{ id, name, lineId, marks, segments, wWind }]` + `activeCalcId`. Building-wide config (code/species/grade/seismic/dead loads) stays in the SHARED `g`; only `wWind` is per-tab (`gEff = {...g, wWind: activeTab.wWind}`; `setGlCalc` routes `wWind`→active tab, everything else→shared `g`; `setSegments` writes the active tab). `applyToCalc(line, segs, res, dC, name, marks)` now CREATES a sub-tab, or — if a tab with the same `line.id` already exists — UPDATES it in place (re-send = refresh, never a duplicate). A per-tab pass/fail dot (`calcTabStatus` memo runs the untouched engine once per tab) shows on each sub-tab. (3) **Name consistency** — the per-segment marks now match across tabs: the Design tab's `wallMarks` for the pushed line ride along as `marks` and the calc-sheet components (`LtSegHeader`/`LtComplianceBanner`/`LtElevation` via a shared `swMark(marks,i)` helper, threaded through `CalcSheet`) render "SW-A/SW-B" instead of "SW-1/SW-2" — identical to the Design tab and globally unique on the plan; a MANUAL tab (no line) falls back to "SW-1/SW-2" unchanged. (4) **"+" add button** — a Chrome-style new-tab button at the end of the sub-tab row creates a blank manual calc (`addCalcTab`), letting a wall be run independently of the Design tab's Optimize. Tabs also close (×, never below 1) and manual tabs rename on double-click. **Persistence:** `calc.tabs`/`calc.activeCalcId` added to the `.wps` save (purely ADDITIVE, feature-detected on load; `loadProject` wraps a legacy `calc.segments`-only file into one tab, pads each tab to 6 segments, falls back a bad `activeCalcId` to the first tab; `calc.segments` is still written = the active tab so a pre-132 build can still open the file). `CURRENT_VERSION` stays 2 (additive). **NO guarded engine fn touched — `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; all 8 app-file guarded fns byte-identical.** Verified: esbuild compile CLEAN (no dup-key warnings); `calcCore.js` byte-identical (diffed vs upload); guarded-fn heads unchanged; SSR App smoke on the calc tab PASS (default "Wall 1" tab + "+" button render); NEW `loadProject` back-compat logic test 14/14 (legacy wrap, v132 restore incl. marks/per-tab wWind/activeCalcId, bad-activeCalcId fallback, no-calc→null); NEW multi-tab SSR test 7/7 (two sub-tabs render with close + add buttons; an active line-derived tab shows SW-C/SW-D from its passed marks, not SW-1). `APP_BUILD = 132` ("Version 1.32"). Prior rev — rev 52 — **STALE-PUSH FOLLOW-UP: a caution sign (⚠) on every stale button + the Design-tab ⚡ Optimize design button now gets the same red/⚠ treatment (user-requested).** Two additions to rev 51. (1) A caution triangle is prefixed to a button's label whenever it is in the red stale state — shared const `WARN = "\u26A0\uFE0E "` (U+FE0E forces the MONOCHROME text triangle, so it inherits the button's red text color rather than the yellow emoji), placed INLINE to the left of the label with a trailing space so it never overlaps/obstructs the text. Wired on all 4 stale buttons (`{designStaleHint && WARN}` on the ribbon ⚡ + side-panel Design buttons, `{calcStaleHint && WARN}` on Send-to-calc). (2) The **⚡ Optimize design** button (in `DesignTab`, runs `optimizeAll`, which PRODUCES the tab's design output) now turns red + ⚠ when an input it consumes has changed since the last Optimize. New module fn `optimizeSig(linesByFloor, lines, twoStory, g, d)` serializes every line's force/height/length/tributary across BOTH floors + `g` + `d`, but EXCLUDES `g.wWind` (optimizeAll overrides it per-line with the line's own force, so a calc-sheet push that sets `g.wWind` must not mark Optimize stale) and `g.line` (cosmetic). State `optimizePush` lives in `App` (not `DesignTab`, which unmounts on a tab switch), reset on New/Open; `optimizeAll` snapshots the sig after designing; `DesignTab` computes `optimizeLiveSig` live and `optimizeStaleHint = optimizePush!=null && optimizePush!==optimizeLiveSig`; the button spreads `STALE_BTN` over its `swBtn(true)` style when stale. A Plan→Design re-push (new lines) → the sig diverges → Optimize goes red, as does editing g/d on the Design tab. **NO guarded fn touched — `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; all 12 guarded fns byte-identical.** Verified: compile CLEAN; engine guard CLEAN (12/12); SSR App smoke PASS (32,384, no premature ⚠/red); preview bundle SSR 32,384; rev-130 logic test 13/13 + NEW `work/_rev130b_optimize.cjs` 13/13 (`optimizeSig` deterministic + sensitive to line force/length, g.species, d.hdDist; INSENSITIVE to g.wWind + g.line; single-story falls back to `lines`; staleHint semantics; caution sign wired on all 4 buttons + the Optimize button) — `WARN` runtime-confirmed = U+26A0 U+FE0E + space. `APP_BUILD = 131` ("Version 1.31"). Prior rev — rev 51 — **STALE-PUSH INDICATOR: a "push data" button turns its text RED when upstream edits would change the downstream tab on re-push (user-requested).** A push-forward button (the Plan→Design **⚡ Design shear walls** button — both the ribbon + side-panel copies — and the Design→Calc **Send line to calculation sheet** button) now masks its text in red once you have pushed AND a later upstream edit would change what a re-push produces; pushing again clears it. Mechanism = a SIGNATURE of the exact push payload captured at push time vs a live signature: Plan→Design snapshots `JSON.stringify(byFloor)` (the design lines) — `runDesignHandoff` was split into a pure `computeHandoff()` (returns `byFloor`, no side effect) + a thin pusher that hands off and sets `pushedSig`; a `liveHandoffSig` memo re-runs `computeHandoff` on every handoff-input change (same deps as before), and `designStaleHint = pushedSig!==null && live!==pushed`. Design→Calc snapshots `calcPushSig(line,segs,res,d)` (segment lengths + force/height/trib + per-seg selType + the seeded `d` fields) keyed to the sent line's id; the Send button is red only when the SELECTED line is the one in the sheet AND its signature has since changed (selecting a different line is a fresh push, not stale). Because the signal is the push payload, pure-view edits (zoom, markup scale, selection, snap/ortho/dims) never trip it and an edit-then-revert clears it. Reset on New/Open (`pushedSig`→null in the sketcher `set()`; `calcPush`→null in onNew/onOpen) — a loaded file is treated as in sync, re-arming on the next push (so editing after Open without pushing won't pre-warn; live-session signal, NOT serialized → no `.wps` schema change). Red look = a shared `STALE_BTN` style (red text `#C0271F`, pale-red wash, red border) applied inline so it overrides each button's base class/style. **NO guarded engine fn touched — `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL; all 8 app-file guarded fns byte-identical (12/12).** Verified: esbuild compile CLEAN; engine guard CLEAN (12/12); SSR App render smoke PASS (32,384 — Plan tab structurally unchanged); single-file preview bundle compiles + SSR-renders to the same 32,384; NEW focused logic test `work/_rev130_stale.cjs` 13/13 (`calcPushSig` determinism + sensitivity to seg/force/hdDist/selType/height/roofTrib + PRECISION: a non-pushed field like `lengthFt` leaves the signature unchanged + edit-then-revert returns to original + staleHint semantics incl. different-line→not-stale). `APP_BUILD = 130` ("Version 1.30"). Prior rev — rev 49 — **DEAD-LOAD TRIBUTARY IS NOW A PER-WALL, PER-FLOOR PLAN INPUT (replaces the global Design-tab Roof/Floor trib boxes).** The user asked to move the Design tab's two DL-tributary inputs onto the plan, because tributary differs wall-to-wall. Prior rev — rev 48 — **STACKED WALLS NOW PAIRED GEOMETRICALLY → the two floors are ONE wall (shared id + geometry; move/stretch together; no floor-switch shift).** Follow-up to rev 47 on the same north wall. Rev 47 paired a stacked wall's two floors BY ID, but they often don't share an id: the collinear-support cluster (≈line 201) keys each line to its LONGEST collinear edge, and for the 1st-floor line that's frequently the 1-STORY portion — so the north wall's 1st-floor line was `ax|1storyKey` while its 2nd-floor line was `ax|2storyKey`. Rev 47's id match missed it, leaving TWO independent lines: the floors didn't share a `segsByLine` entry (length/position edits on one floor never reached the other) and centered in different spans (the wall shifted from the 2-story-segment center to the full-wall center on a floor switch), and the rev-47 stacked optimizer/stacking never even engaged for it. Fix — pair the floors **geometrically** in `runDesignHandoff`: each 2nd-floor line adopts the collinear 1st-floor line (same orientation + wind axis + fixed coordinate) whose span tightest-contains the 2-story segment; that 1st-floor line then TAKES the 2nd floor's id + extent (id/key/a/b/lengthFt) while KEEPING its own 1st-floor reaction + design height. Both floors now share ONE id (one segments array → they move + stretch together like any other wall) and ONE geometry (centered identically, confined to the 2-story segment), which also makes the rev-47 stacking + 1st-floor-controlled optimizer actually engage for the north wall. Uniform 2-story walls coincide → pairing is identity; 1-story-only lines find no 2-story partner → untouched. **Engine guard intact: `calcCore.js` BYTE-IDENTICAL** (verified) — geometry/handoff logic only; no formula, schedule, or `.wps` schema change (paired geometry regenerates on every handoff). **Verified:** TS-parser syntax + dup-key scan CLEAN; `calcCore.js` byte-identical; full harness NOT run (no engine change). `APP_BUILD = 127` ("Version 1.27"). User previews a mixed building: the north wall's 1st & 2nd floor shear walls are now the SAME wall — drag/stretch on either floor updates both, and switching floors shows it in the SAME place (no shift). Prior rev — rev 47 — **MIXED-HEIGHT STACKED WALLS: ALIGNED TO THE 2-STORY SEGMENT + 1ST-FLOOR-CONTROLLED OPTIMIZATION.** Two user-reported structural issues on the Design tab for a mixed 2-story+1-story wall (the "north wall"). **(1) Alignment:** the two floors of a stacked wall were drawn out of sync and the 2nd-floor wall could overflow its line. Cause — a stacked wall's 1st-floor line spans the FULL wall (built on the full graph) while its 2nd-floor line spans only the 2-story sub-segment (built on `twoStoryGraph`, which drops 1-story edges); both floors share ONE segment array (by id) drawn anchored to each floor's own `ln.a`, so different origins/lengths desynced the stack. Fix — in `runDesignHandoff`, after building both floors, the 1st-floor line now ADOPTS its 2nd-floor partner's extent (`a`/`b`/`lengthFt` = the 2-story segment) while KEEPING its own 1st-floor reaction + design height; both floors share one origin + bound, so segments stack/align and ALL placement (drag, add, optimize) is confined to the 2-story segment (per the user: the 1-story portion gets no shear wall of its own on this line). Uniform 2-story walls already match → no-op. **(2) Optimization now 1st-floor-controlled:** the old optimizer scored candidates only with single-floor `calcSegment`, so it picked the shortest wall the LIGHTER 2nd floor allowed (e.g. 6 ft) and forced that length onto the 1st floor, where the combined overturning could exhaust the largest holdown/post → FAIL. New app-side `generateStackedDesign(line1,line2,g,d)` mirrors `generateDesign`'s (N,Ls) search but scores every candidate through the SAME validators the tab displays — `stackedLineResults` (1st-floor arm-aware combined demand) AND the 2nd floor's own `lineResults` — and returns the shortest layout that passes BOTH, bounded by the 2-story segment. So the heavier 1st floor governs and the wall is free to grow (e.g. 10 ft) when 6 ft can't pass; that one length is reused on the 2nd floor. If nothing passes within the segment it returns null → the line reports FAIL (never spills past the segment, per the user's call). `optimizeAll` now routes stacked pairs (a wall on BOTH floors) to `generateStackedDesign` and 1-story-only / single-story lines to the standalone `generateDesign`, still merging across floors (rev 46). **Engine guard intact: `calcCore.js` is BYTE-IDENTICAL** (diffed vs the upload) — the stacked optimizer only composes its exported primitives via `lineResults`/`stackSeg`; no formula touched. This closes the rev-46 §7 "optimizer uses the per-floor reaction, not the stacked demand" gap for stacked walls. **Verified:** TS-parser syntax + dup-key scan CLEAN; `calcCore.js` byte-identical; full harness NOT run (no engine change; re-run §6/§6b at next session start). `APP_BUILD = 126` ("Version 1.26"). User previews a mixed building: Optimize once → the north wall's 1st & 2nd floors show the SAME aligned shear wall within the 2-story segment, sized by the 1st floor (can exceed the 2nd-floor-only length). Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. See §4vv. Prior rev — rev 46 — **DESIGN TAB: OPTIMIZE NOW DESIGNS BOTH FLOORS + MERGES (fixes a mixed 2-story+1-story wall vanishing/FAILing on a Level 1↔2 switch).** User-reported bug: in a mixed 2-story + 1-story building, after ⚡ Optimize design, switching between Level 1 and Level 2 made a wall's shear wall DISAPPEAR and show a FAIL badge until you clicked Optimize again. Root cause: `optimizeAll` (in `DesignTab`) built a fresh `next` object from ONLY the currently-viewed floor's `lines` and then did `setSegsByLine(next)` — a **wholesale replace that DROPPED the segments of every line not on the viewed floor.** Because the two floors have different line sets (Level 2 = `twoStoryGraph` excludes the 1-story walls — §4kk), optimizing on one floor wiped the other floor's layouts; a wall present only on the floor you switched TO then had `segsByLine[id] = undefined → []`, and an empty line draws no wall AND fails the `rs.length>0` pass test (`lineResults([]) → []`), i.e. it "disappeared + failed." Re-optimizing on the now-current floor refilled it. **Fix (display/handoff state only — engine untouched):** `optimizeAll` now designs EVERY wall across BOTH floors via the `linesByFloor` prop (`[...byFloor[1], ...byFloor[2]]`), **deduped by id to the GOVERNING floor** (max `forceLbs`, then max `heightFt`) since a 2-story wall shares one id (`ax|key`) and one segment layout across both floors — so the shared layout is sized for the heavier story — and **MERGES** onto the existing `segsByLine` (`{...segsByLine, ...}`) instead of replacing it, so no floor's layouts are ever wiped. One Optimize click now designs the whole building; switching floors never reveals an un-optimized wall. The status message counts unique walls (`byId.size`) instead of the viewed floor's line count. `onDesignShearWalls` already preserved the cross-floor union (it was never the culprit); the floor toggle only sets `activeFloor`. NO guarded engine / `calcCore.js` / wind / `.wps` schema change; `generateDesign`/`lineResults`/`stackedLineResults` untouched (the optimizer still sizes from each line's own `forceLbs` — the pre-existing "optimizer uses the per-floor reaction, not the arm-aware stacked demand" gap is unchanged and noted in §7). **Verified:** TS-parser syntax + dup-key scan CLEAN; engine guard NOT run this session (no engine touch; user asked not to run the harness) — re-run §6/§6b at next session start. `APP_BUILD = 125` ("Version 1.25"). Prior rev — rev 43 — **MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY — SECTION CUT DIAPHRAGMS NOW CONNECT TO EACH WALL'S TOP + DEFORM ON HEIGHT EDIT (like the 1-story).** The user asked to bring two behaviors of the original 1-story `SecDiagram` into the mixed `SecDiagramSeq`: (1) editing a wall's pressure/height updates the Level 1 / Level 2 diaphragm values, and (2) the nodes are connected so changing a wall height makes the shape DEFORM (the 1-story draws a sloping ROOF LINE between the two wall tops). Fix (display/UI only — guarded engine byte-identical): the Level-1 (floor) diaphragm is now a **polyline through every wall's own 1st-story top** (`floorY(i)=wallBot−H·pxPerFt`) with a NODE at each, and the Level-2 (roof) diaphragm is a **polyline through the 2-story block walls' full tops** (`roofY(i)=wallBot−(H+H₂)·pxPerFt`) with nodes — exactly the 1-story's sloping roof line generalized to N walls. Prior rev — rev 34 — **FLOOR DIAPHRAGM NO LONGER DOUBLE-COUNTS THE ROOF LOAD (2-story section-cut + plan display fix; user-requested).** In 2-story mode the 2nd-floor (level-2) diaphragm line load was being shown as ½·H·pw + ½·H₂·pw + **roof diaphragm** (e.g. 104+104+374 = **582 plf**). > **rev 44 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · LEEWARD-MOST WALL HEIGHT EDITABLE (geometry-only) + DEFAULT WALL HEIGHT 10ft (user-requested).** Two fixes. (1) The user noted that the 1-story section cut lets you edit the leeward wall's height (for correct geometry) even though that wall has no load, and asked for the same on the mixed section cut's LAST wall in the wind direction. (2) Make the default wall height 10ft and parapet 5ft.
> - **Leeward-most wall height editable.** `SecDiagramSeq`'s back-box group previously rendered only when the back wall had a parapet (`w.par>0`) and exposed only `qLee` + parapet height — the wall's HEIGHT was fixed. It now ALWAYS renders an `H` box (`field="leeH" prop="leeH"` → `upd` → `setVals("lee",{H})`) and, when the back wall is 2-story (Section C), an `H₂` box (`leeH2` → `setVals("lee",{H2})`); the parapet pressure/height boxes stay gated on `par>0`. `propOf(last)` already read `v.leeH`/`v.leeH2`, and the open-section seed already populates them from the leeward partner — so editing the box flows into the rev-43 connected diaphragm polyline and the leeward wall redraws/deforms (its top node moves), exactly like the 1-story's editable `HR` tilting the roof line. The leeward wall carries no diaphragm load, so this is geometry-only: it routes through `upd`/`"lee"` (NOT the interior `commit` path) and does NOT change the Level-1/Level-2 load values — same as the 1-story, where `wallRes` uses the windward `HL` and `HR` only sets the roof slope.
> - **Default wall height 10ft.** `DEF_SECTION.H: 13 → 10` (parapet already 5; H₂ is null → equals H, so a new wall is H=10, H₂=10, par=5). VALUE-only change — no schema field renamed/added/removed, so the load-state schema tripwire (locks field NAMES) is unaffected; re-run `test_schema.cjs` to confirm and, only if it also snapshots default values, update `schema.expected.json` (intentional change). Existing saved `.wps` files keep their stored heights (merge only fills MISSING keys), so this affects NEW walls only.

> **rev 43 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · SECTION-CUT DIAPHRAGMS CONNECT TO EACH WALL'S TOP + DEFORM ON HEIGHT EDIT (user-requested; ports two 1-story behaviors).** The user asked to make the mixed section cut (`SecDiagramSeq`) behave like the original 1-story `SecDiagram` in two ways: (1) changing a wall's pressure/height updates the Level 1 / Level 2 diaphragm values; (2) the nodes are connected so changing a wall height deforms the shape (the 1-story draws a sloping ROOF LINE polygon between the windward + leeward wall tops, with node circles that reposition live). Study of `SecDiagram`: it reads all geometry from the live `v` buffer (`roofYL=wallBot−HL·pxPerFt`, `roofYR=wallBot−HR·pxPerFt`), draws the wall as a trapezoid whose top edge is the roof line, and the line load value reads `v` too — so both behaviors fall out of "draw from the live values + connect the tops."
> - **Root cause (2).** `SecDiagramSeq` drew the floor diaphragm as ONE flat `<line>` at `yF2 = wallBot − max(H)·pxPerFt` and the roof diaphragm as one flat `<line>` at `yRoof = wallBot − max(H+H₂)·pxPerFt`, with each wall an independent vertical. So a non-tallest wall's top sat BELOW the flat diaphragm (a gap) and editing its height moved only that stub — nothing "connected," and the pinned-flat look made height edits read as inert.
> - **Fix.** New per-wall levels `floorY(i)=wallBot−W[i].H·pxPerFt` (1st-story top) and `roofY(i)=wallBot−(W[i].H+(one?0:H₂))·pxPerFt` (full top). The Level-1 diaphragm is now `<polyline>` through `floorY(i)` for ALL walls + a node `<circle>` at each; the Level-2 diaphragm is a `<polyline>` through `roofY(i)` over the block (`twoIdx`) + nodes. Each wall's top coincides with its diaphragm node, so they connect; change any H/H₂ and the node moves → the diaphragm slopes/steps → the section deforms as one connected shape (the 1-story sloping roof, generalized to N walls). When all heights match, the polylines are flat == the old look (uniform building unchanged). The value callouts anchor to the diaphragm's leeward end (`cFloorY=floorY(last)`, `cRoofY=roofY(block last)`) so they ride the slope; the parapet-start node moved to the parapet TOP (`pty`) so it doesn't double-draw over a diaphragm node.
> - **Behaviour (1) — already live, now confirmed + visible.** `WindWindow` computes `floorLLmix`/`roofLLseq` from `section.seq` and `v` in its render body, and `activeSection.seq` is recomputed from `propsFor` (=`wallProps`) every App render — so a block-wall edit (interior `commit` → `wallProps`) or a front/back edit (`v`/`upd`, which also writes `wallProps`) flows straight into the values. Editing a block wall's H₂/pw raises Level 1 (the poured-forward ½·H₂·pw `seqAcc`) AND Level 2 (the block's ½·H₂·pw); parapet edits raise the parapet terms. The leeward wall's HEIGHT changes only the SHAPE (now visibly, via the polyline) and not the load value — exactly like the 1-story, where the leeward `HR` tilts the roof line but `wallRes` uses the windward `HL`.
>
> `SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded wind + shear-wall engines untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular ≡ inlined preview). rev-41 + rev-42 regressions still 8/8. NEW **`work/_rev43_connect.cjs`** PASSES 10/10: the floor diaphragm is a 4-point polyline that slopes to a short leeward wall (connected, deforms); the roof diaphragm is a 2-point polyline that slopes when the block's H₂ differ; ≥6 connection nodes; a uniform building → FLAT floor diaphragm (no regression); and the Level-2 value rises 404→484 when the block H₂ goes 10→20 and →474 when the block pw goes 16→30 (height AND pressure edits update the values). `APP_BUILD = 123` ("Version 1.23"). Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. See §4rr.

> **rev 42 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · INTERIOR BLOCK WALLS NOW FULLY EDITABLE — height + pressure (user-requested).** The user asked to remove the rev-41 limitation: the 2-story BLOCK walls drawn in the middle of the mixed section cut (`SecDiagramSeq`) were display-only, so their height/pressure couldn't be changed — "the walls need to be as editable as the rest of the walls." Now every wall the cut crosses is editable. Display/UI change only — the guarded engine and every formula are byte-identical.
> - **Generalized `setVals` (parent).** `setVals(target, patch)` already mapped `"self"` → the active (windward) wall and `"lee"` → its leeward partner. Added one branch — `else if(target && target!=="self") key=target` — so an explicit EDGE KEY edits that exact wall's `wallProps`. Backward-compatible: `"self"`/`"lee"` behave as before, and real wall keys (from `keyOf`) never equal those literals.
> - **`WindWindow` → `SecDiagramSeq`.** Passes `commit={(key,prop,val)=>setVals(key,{[prop]:val})}`. Front/back editing keeps its existing `v`/`upd` path (which already persisted to `wallProps`); `commit` is only used by the new interior boxes.
> - **`SecDiagramSeq` editing made key-aware.** New `commit` prop; a per-wall raw-string buffer `ebuf` keyed `"${key}:${prop}"` (so typing "13." isn't collapsed to 13 mid-keystroke); `open(field,prop,cx,cy,key)` now carries an optional edge key and `Box` forwards a `wkey`; a `seqVal(key,prop)` reader for the current value; and a new group of editable boxes on the interior block ends. The block FRONT wall (windward face, drawn only when `bw!==0`) gets `pw` · `H` · `H₂` · `par` · `qWind`; the block BACK wall (leeward face, `bl!==last`) gets `qLee` · `par` · `H` · `H₂` — the same set the front/back already expose. The gates `bw!==0`/`bl!==last` ensure a block end that IS the sequence front/back keeps its original front/back boxes (no double box). The floating input branches on `edit.key`: keyed → value `= ebuf["key:prop"] ?? String(seqVal(key,prop))`, `onChange` writes `ebuf` + `commit(key,prop,num(raw))`, `onBlur` clears that `ebuf` entry; unkeyed → the existing `v`/`upd` path. Enter/Escape now blur (so the keyed path's buffer cleanup runs).
> - **Why values stay live with no extra wiring.** A keyed edit writes `wallProps[key]`; `propsFor` is derived from `wallProps`, and `activeSection.seq` (hence `section.seq` in `WindWindow`) recomputes from `propsFor` on every render. `roofLLseq`, the floor accumulation `seqAcc`, and `SecDiagramSeq`'s own `propOf(interior)` all already read from `seq` — so editing a block wall's `H₂`/`pw`/parapet flows straight into the Level-2 diaphragm value, the Level-1 accumulation, and the drawn arrows, exactly like a front/back edit. (Front/back edits go through `v` and also write `wallProps`, so the two paths stay consistent.)
>

(The test needs `globalThis.IS_REACT_ACT_ENVIRONMENT=true`, `React.act`, and a FRESH box re-query each iteration — `setEdit` re-renders the SVG and replaces the `<g>` nodes, so a once-captured node list goes stale; the app code was correct, the harness needed the re-query.) `APP_BUILD = 122` ("Version 1.22"). > **rev 41 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · SECTION CUT DRAWS THE LEVEL-2 (ROOF) PRESSURES + VALUE; DIAPHRAGMS RENAMED LEVEL 1 / LEVEL 2 (user-requested).** Three things the user flagged on the rev-40 mixed section cut (`SecDiagramSeq`), comparing it to the CAD schematic (SECTION A / SECTION C): the diagram drew the 2-story block as bare lines so the pressures that *generate* the upper diaphragm were missing; the upper-diaphragm VALUE wasn't shown (just "→ block's own walls"); and the diaphragm callout text overlapped the leeward wall line. Plus a rename request: call them "Level 1 / Level 2" instead of "floor / roof". All DISPLAY-only — the guarded engine and every load value are byte-identical.
> - **Block pressures drawn.** New draw group in `SecDiagramSeq` over the 2-story block: the front-most 2-story wall (`bw=twoIdx[0]`) gets WINDWARD pressure — `pw` arrows over its UPPER story (roof→floor of the block; the lower story is shadowed by whatever is in front of it) + `qWind` arrows over its parapet — and the back-most 2-story wall (`bl=twoIdx[last]`) gets its LEEWARD parapet (`qLee`, arrows to the right). Gated `bw!==0` / `bl!==last` so a block end that IS the editable sequence front/back (Section C / C-reverse) isn't drawn twice — the existing front-windward / back-leeward draw already covers it. Arrow lengths come from a new `aOf(psf)` helper and the arrow scale `maxPsf` now spans every wall's `pw/qWind/qLee` so the block arrows are proportional. This mirrors the schematic exactly: windward 1-story wall, block front (32 parapet + 16 upper), block back (22 parapet), leeward 1-story wall.
> - **Level-2 (roof) value shown.** `WindWindow` computes `roofLLseq` = `½·H₂·pw + windward parapet + leeward parapet` of the block — the SAME shape as the uniform-two-story `roofLL`, but read from the block's front/back `seq` walls (front → `qWind`, back → `qLee`), with live-`v` substitution where a block end coincides with the editable sequence front/back. Passed into `SecDiagramSeq` as a `roofLL` prop and rendered in the upper callout (replacing "→ block's own walls"); also added to the breakdown panel as a "Level 2 diaphragm line load → designs the level-2 (2-story block) walls" section with `½·H₂·pw (block, upper ½)` + `windward + leeward parapet (block)` sub-rows. In the schematic's 10ft/16psf + 6ft/32+22psf case → `½·10·16 + 6·32 + 6·22 = 404 plf`.
> - **Rename → Level 1 / Level 2.** Every user-facing "roof diaphragm" → **"Level 2 diaphragm"** and "floor / 2nd-floor diaphragm" → **"Level 1 diaphragm"**, in `SecDiagramSeq`, `SecDiagram2`, and both breakdown panels (`mixedSeq` and `twoStoryView`); the "designs Nth-floor shear walls" sublabels became "designs the level-N (upper/lower) shear walls". **Naming implication examined:** the mapping is unambiguous — naming a diaphragm by the STORY it designs (roof→level-2 walls, floor→level-1 walls) AND naming it by its own ELEVATION (the lower/first diaphragm = Level 1, the upper/second = Level 2) both give roof = Level 2, floor = Level 1. The change is confined to displayed strings + the comments at the label sites; the `roofLL`/`floorLL`/`roofLLseq`/`floorLLmix` VARIABLE names are intentionally KEPT (with a mapping comment at their definitions) to hold the diff tight and avoid churn near the guarded-engine-adjacent code — no value, engine, load-path, reaction, or design-handoff change. (If the user ever wants the identifiers renamed too, it's a mechanical follow-up.)
> - **Overlap fix.** viewBox `VBW 362→380`, wall span pulled left (`rightX 284→250`), callouts moved to `calloutX=300` — now right of the leeward wall (250) + its arrows (≤30 → 280), so the "Level 1/Level 2 diaphragm … plf" text no longer sits on the wall line.
>

> **rev 40 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · SEQUENCE-BASED OVERALL SECTION CUT (A/B/C/C-reverse).** The user flagged two things on the rev-39 section cut: it changed between the 1st- and 2nd-floor plans (it should be ONE overall-building section), and Section C rendered like Section A. Root causes: (a) the open-section `useEffect` resolved the windward wall from the floor-filtered `secH/secV`, so on the 2nd floor the 1-story windward wall was missing and a different wall anchored the section; (b) `SecDiagramMix` only ever drew "1-story front + one 2-story block + 1-story back", so any cut ending on a 2-story wall (Section C) still drew a closing 1-story wall (Section A). Both fixed by switching to a SEQUENCE model:
> - **`sectionSequence(sAcross, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)`** (module fn, after `nearestTwoStoryBehind`) — returns the ordered list of every across-wind (`recv`) wall whose span includes the cut's across-wind position `sAcross`, sorted by downwind depth (windward→leeward), each `{key, one, H, H2, par, pw, qWind, qLee, depth}`. Always the FULL graph → floor-independent. The 1/2-story pattern IS the section type: `1·2·2·1`=A, `1·1`=B, `1·2·2`=C, `2·2·1`=C-reverse.
> - **Floor independence** — the open-section `useEffect` now computes `seq = sectionSequence(po.sAcross, …full graph…)` and sets `activeWall.key = seq[0].key` (the true windward wall) instead of falling back to the filtered `sc.windLoads[0]`. So the SAME wall anchors the section on either floor. `activeSection` also carries `seq` (recomputed from `activeWall.sAcross`, or the wall's center as a fallback).
> - **`SecDiagramSeq({seq,v,upd,floorLL})`** REPLACES `SecDiagramMix`. Draws N walls evenly spaced front→back, each at its own height (1-story green to `H`+parapet, 2-story dark to `H+H₂`+parapet); the floor diaphragm dashes across ALL walls at the 1-story top, the roof diaphragm spans the contiguous 2-story block (`twoIdx`); windward pressure on the front wall (full height+parapet), leeward pressure on the back; front & back walls editable via the live `v`/`upd` buffer (incl. an H₂ box when the front wall is 2-story, for C-reverse), interior walls display-only. Handles all 4 types from the sequence alone — no per-type branching.
> - **`WindWindow`** — `seq = section.seq||[]`; `hasOne/hasTwo`; `mixedSeq = twoStory && hasOne && hasTwo && seq.length>=2`. Diagram: `mixedSeq ? <SecDiagramSeq> : twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2> : <SecDiagram>`. The floor-diaphragm line load = `seqBase + seqLeePar + seqAcc` where `seqBase = ½·H·pw + (front 1-story ? windPar : 0)`, `seqAcc = front 1-story ? ½·H₂·pw of the nearest 2-story in the sequence : ½·H₂·pw of the front wall itself`, `seqLeePar` counted only if the BACK wall is 1-story — matching `buildSecDataF1`. Breakdown panel shows ½·H·pw + parapets + the poured-forward ½·H₂·pw (= 478 in the user's H₂=13 case). Section B (all 1-story) → `SecDiagram`; uniform 2-story → `SecDiagram2`; both unchanged.
> 
> `SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded wind/shear-wall engines are untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12); compile clean; render smoke PASS (32,149). NEW **`work/test_step5.cjs`** PASSES: `sectionSequence` returns `[1,2,2,1]`/`[1,1]`/`[1,2,2]`/`[2,2,1]` for A/B/C/C-reverse, is floor-independent (no floor input), and `SecDiagramSeq` draws the right number of 1-STY/2-STY markers (A: 2+2, C: 1+2) with C-reverse's front wall designing a 2-story wall. (`test_step4b.cjs` from rev 39 was retired — it asserted on the removed `SecDiagramMix`.) Steps 2/3/4 regressions pass. `APP_BUILD = 120` ("Version 1.20"). **Drawing proportions/labels are a first pass pending the user's eyeball — all contained in `SecDiagramSeq`.** Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. See §4oo.

> **rev 39 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · STEPPED SECTION CUT (user follow-up to Step 4).** The user noted the Step-4 section cut "doesn't look like the schematics": a 1-story cut drew a flat single-story elevation, but the schematic SECTION A (the 454) is a *stepped* section — the 1-story windward wall AND the 2-story block standing behind it (the source of the +80). The current windward+leeward section model never drew that in-between block. This rev adds it. **`nearestTwoStoryBehind(key, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)`** (module fn) mirrors `buildSecDataF1`'s `backs` scan to find the nearest 2-story `recv`-orientation wall downwind of the windward wall, returning its props (or null). `activeSection.behind` is set to that (only when the cut wall `isOneStory`). New component **`SecDiagramMix`** draws the stepped elevation: short green 1-story windward wall + parapet (left), the taller dark 2-story block behind it rising to its roof (with H₂ shown display-only), the green leeward wall (right), the floor-diaphragm line across the 1-story tops, a roof-diaphragm callout over the block ("→ block's own walls"), and the windward/leeward fields stay editable via the same `upd` mechanism. **`WindWindow`** computes `behind = section.behind`, `accBehind = ½·H₂·pw`, `mixedStep = oneStory && behind`, `floorLLmix = wallRes + windPar + leePar + accBehind` (= 454), and routes: `mixedStep ? <SecDiagramMix…> : twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2…> : <SecDiagram…>`, with a matching 454 floor-diaphragm breakdown panel (this 1-story wall's ½·H·pw + windward&leeward parapet + the poured-forward ½·H₂·pw). A 1-story wall with nothing 2-story behind → still the plain single-story window; pure 2-story cuts → `SecDiagram2` unchanged; `SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded engine untouched. **Verification:** engine guard CLEAN (12/12), compile clean, render smoke PASS (32,149), Steps 2/3/4 regressions PASS, NEW `work/test_step4b.cjs` PASSES (`nearestTwoStoryBehind` returns the box with H₂=10 behind the windward perimeter wall; `WindWindow` SSR routes a 1-story+behind cut to the stepped diagram showing the "2-STORY"/"BEHIND" block + the "2-story portion behind" breakdown term + "Floor diaphragm line load", and NOT the 2-story roof/floor split; a 1-story+nothing-behind cut shows the plain "Total wall line load"). `APP_BUILD = 119` ("Version 1.19"). **The stepped diagram is a first cut built to match SECTION A from the schematic — its exact proportions/labels are pending the user's eyeball in the preview and are easy to tune (it's one self-contained component).** Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. > **rev 38 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · STEP 4/4 (FINAL): SECTION CUTS + HANDOFF FINALIZE — FEATURE COMPLETE.** A wall tagged 1-story now cuts as a SINGLE-story elevation. The section-cut window (`WindWindow`) gained an `oneStory` prop, set at the invocation to `isOneStory(activeWall.key)`; inside, a derived `twoStoryView = twoStory && !oneStory` replaces `twoStory` in BOTH the diagram routing (`twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2 …roofLL floorLL/> : <SecDiagram/>`) and the line-load breakdown routing (roof+floor split vs. the single "Total wall line load"). > **rev 37 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · STEP 3/4: 1ST-FLOOR (FLOOR DIAPHRAGM) ACCUMULATION — "THE 454".** On the 1st-floor view + floor-1 design of a building with ≥1 tagged 1-story wall, a windward wall's floor-diaphragm plf VARIES along its length: each across-wind sub-region sums the strips connected to the FLOOR diaphragm in its downwind shadow, so the front wall splits into regions (the user's worked example: `32×5 + 16×13/2 + 22×5 = 374` where nothing two-story is behind it, `+ 16×10/2 = 454` where the box is). Matches the "1ST FLOOR PLAN" schematic; the dashed tributary divide is drawn at each 454/374 boundary. **New additive fn `buildSecDataF1(section, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor, isOne)`** — a focused copy of `buildSecData` (same windward + overlap-shadow + line-grouping + back-wall-subdivision machinery; reuses `findLeewardPartner` and `lineReactions` verbatim) with the floor-1 mixed load rule swapped in. Per windward wall the sub-region plf = `base + leePar·qLee + acc` where: `base` = ½·H·pw + (1-story ? own parapet·qWind : ½·H₂·pw of its own upper wall); `leePar` = the exterior (farthest-downwind) back wall's parapet but ONLY if that back wall is 1-story (a 2-story back wall's parapet belongs to the roof diaphragm); `acc` = ½·H₂·pw of the NEAREST 2-story back wall covering the sub-region (ONE face — the bottom half of its upper wall; its top half already went to the roof). Back walls are gathered exactly like `buildSecData`'s `backs` (downwind, `recv` orientation, overlapping across-wind), now tagged with `{par (if 1-story), h2 (if 2-story), d}`; breakpoints at their lo/hi split the windward span → the 454/374 regions. **Wiring:** `mixed1 = twoStory && activeFloor===1 && oneStory.size>0`; the live `secH`/`secV` call `buildSecDataF1(sections.*, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor /*RAW, not propsForActive*/, isOneStory)` when `mixed1`, else `buildSecData` as before; `buildFloor(1)` does the same via a local `mixedF1`. The rev-34 `displayPlf` override (`floorDiaphragmPlf`) and the `divides` hide are both re-gated `…&&!mixed1`, so the mixed wall shows its true per-region 454/374 labels + divides, while a uniform 2-story building (no tags) is byte-identical to rev 36. **Why a sibling fn, not an edit:** the floor-1 mixed model differs structurally (the front wall accumulates a deeper wall's load, and parapets route by wall type) — and the guarded `buildSecData` must stay byte-identical; a copy keeps both. **Verification:** engine guard CLEAN (12/12), esbuild compile clean, SSR render smoke PASS (32,149), Step-2 regression PASS, and new checked-in **`work/test_step3.cjs`** runs the REAL bundled `buildSecDataF1` on a 1-story-perimeter + 2-story-box fixture and asserts the windward wall's sub-regions are exactly `[374,374,454]`, `Δ = ½·H₂·pw = 80`, the **middle third over the box carries 454**, the box walls are NOT separately loaded (shadowed → accumulated forward), and a divide is emitted. `APP_BUILD = 117` ("Version 1.17"). Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED. See §4ll. Remaining: Step 4 (section cuts + handoff finalize).

> **rev 36 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · STEP 2/4: 2ND-FLOOR (ROOF DIAPHRAGM) EXCLUDES 1-STORY WALLS.** The tag now changes behavior. On the **2nd-floor** plan + design, a 1-story (green) wall no longer exists for the roof diaphragm: it collects no line load, casts no overlap-shadow, and takes no point-load reaction — only the two-story walls carry the roof and form its lateral system (matches the user's "2nd floor plan" schematic; the live metrics' base shear drops accordingly). The **1st-floor** view and **1-story mode** are untouched (Step 3 handles floor 1). **Implementation — the guarded engine is byte-identical; it simply receives a filtered graph:** new memo `twoStoryGraph` = `{edges: graph.edges.filter(e=>!oneStory.has(keyOf(e))), nodes: graph.nodes that those edges still use}` (empty `oneStory` or 1-story mode → returns `graph` itself, so untagged buildings are unchanged); new memo `twoStoryLoop = loopInfo(twoStoryGraph.nodes, twoStoryGraph.edges)` (the box closes into its own ring → exact exterior normals, even though the full perimeter+box graph has `loop===null`). The render path picks `secGraph/secLoop = (twoStory&&activeFloor===2) ? twoStoryGraph/twoStoryLoop : graph/loop` and feeds them to the existing `buildSecData`; `secH`/`secV` deps updated. The design handoff's `buildFloor(floor)` gained `fg/fl` locals (= filtered graph/loop when `twoStory&&floor===2`) used for its `buildSecData` calls, the reaction-edge lookup, and the support-extent scan; `runDesignHandoff` deps gained `twoStoryGraph`/`twoStoryLoop`. **Why graph-filtering, not prop-zeroing:** the engine's `overlapShadow` test would let a 1-story wall sitting in FRONT of the box wrongly shadow (drop) the box's windward wall; removing the wall from the graph entirely is the clean fix and needs no engine edit. **Walls still all RENDER** off the full `graph` (green 1-story walls are drawn, just load-less on floor 2). > **rev 35 — MIXED-HEIGHT TWO-STORY · STEP 1/4: ONE-STORY WALL TAGGING (user-requested, multi-step in progress).** Goal of the whole feature: model buildings that are two-story overall but where some walls/portions are only one story (single-story or open-to-above) — e.g. a 2-story box inside a 1-story perimeter (see the user's schematics). A one-story wall is a diaphragm-connectivity statement: it touches the **floor** diaphragm (its parapet + top-half + own roof at the floor level) and the **foundation**, but never the **roof** diaphragm. **Step 1 is the tag + appearance ONLY** — zero load/analysis change, so a building with no tags is byte-identical to rev 34. Landed this rev: (1) **state** `oneStory` = a `Set` of edge keys, declared beside `noSupport`; (2) **toggle** `toggleOneStory(edge)`; (3) **menu** a new wall right-click item "↧ Switch to 1-story / ↥ Switch to 2-story", rendered ONLY when `twoStory` (sits between "Takes point load" and "Add node here"); (4) **appearance** tagged walls stroke green `C_ONESTORY="#2E6B4F"` via `isOneStory(key)=twoStory&&oneStory.has(key)` — the dashed/dimmed non-load-bearing style still composes on top; (5) **split migration** a split one-story wall passes the tag to both halves (mirrors the `noSupport` line); (6) **persistence** `oneStory:[...]` rides in the `.wps` SKETCHER SESSION `get()`/`set()` (old files → empty Set; NOT part of loadProject's schema, so the schema tripwire is unaffected — same treatment as `noSupport`/`markScale`); (7) **warning** an amber top-right corner overlay `⚠ All walls are 1-story — the 2nd floor has no walls`, gated on `allOneStory = twoStory && edges.length>0 && edges.every(oneStory.has)` (new `.allonestory-warn` CSS, mirrors `.floorbadge`). **NO guarded engine fn touched** — all 12 (`findLeewardPartner`/`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`lineResults`/`stackSeg`/`stackedLineResults`/`upliftStk`/`withUtil` + `calcSegment`/`generateDesign`/`baseDesignSeg`/`evaluateCandidate`) extract-and-diff identical to the rev-34 baseline. Verified: esbuild compile clean (pre-existing dup-key warning only), SSR render smoke PASS (32,149 chars), engine guard CLEAN. **The agreed 4-step plan** (built incrementally, user previews each before the next, like the original two-story feature): **Step 1 (done)** tagging foundation · **Step 2** 2nd-floor (roof-diaphragm) exclusion — hand `buildSecData` a FILTERED graph containing only the two-story walls, so 1-story walls collect no load / cast no shadow / take no reaction up there (engine untouched) · **Step 3** 1st-floor accumulation — the **454**: a windward wall's floor-diaphragm plf VARIES along its length, picking up ½·H₂·pw from any two-story wall standing behind it (a NEW wind fn that extends the existing back-wall subdivision pattern; reuses `lineReactions`; engine untouched) · **Step 4** section cuts (1-story wall cuts as a single-story elevation; asymmetric 1-story-front/2-story-back) + design handoff (floor-2 on filtered graph, floor-1 with accumulation; 1-story floor-1 lines stay unstacked) + finalize. **Confirmed spec** (locked with the user before coding): accumulation = ½·H₂·pw, one face; one-story parapets→floor diaphragm, two-story parapets→roof diaphragm; the two-story region is assumed to CLOSE into a loop (freestanding box is exact; an open set falls back to the centroid-normal heuristic) — v1 acceptable; rev-34's floor-only display stays valid (that was the uniform-2-story special case where the only parapet is at the roof). `APP_BUILD = 115` ("Version 1.15"). > **rev 34 — FLOOR DIAPHRAGM STOPS DOUBLE-COUNTING THE ROOF LOAD (display fix, user-requested).** The 2-story load-path display was wrong: the 2nd-floor diaphragm line load was rendered as `wallRes + wallRes2 + roofLL` (½·H·pw + ½·H₂·pw + the whole roof diaphragm incl. parapets) — i.e. it poured the roof load into the floor diaphragm. Physically the roof diaphragm dumps into the 2nd-story shear wall, which transfers down into the 1st-story shear wall as a POINT load; the floor diaphragm only spans the half-walls above/below it. So the displayed floor diaphragm is now FLOOR-ONLY: `floorLL = wallRes + wallRes2` (= ½·H·pw + ½·H₂·pw; 104+104 = **208 plf** for the H=H₂=13, pw=16 example, vs the old 582). **Edits (all DISPLAY-only, all outside the guarded engine):** (1) `WindWindow`: `floorLL` formula drops `+ roofLL`, and the "roof load transferred ↓" breakdown `<div>` is removed; the section-cut big number and the `SecDiagram2` gold "2nd-flr diaphragm" callout both read `floorLL`, so both update. (2) New `floorDiaphragmPlf = useCallback(key => 0.5·pw·(H+H₂))` next to `propsForActive`, using the REAL (un-substituted) `propsFor` H/H₂. The leeward-parapet term cancels (it's only in the roof), so the floor value is uniform along a wall. (3) `WindLoad` gains a `displayPlf` prop: when non-null it renders ONE span (wa→wb) at that plf instead of the per-region coalesced subLoads; passed only when `twoStory && activeFloor===1`. (4) The dashed tributary `divides` render is gated off when `twoStory && activeFloor===1` (uniform floor load → no within-wall divide). **UNCHANGED on purpose (the point loads must keep stacking):** `propsForActive` (1st floor stays `H_eff = H + 2·H₂`), `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`, `findLeewardPartner`, `secH`/`secV`, `runDesignHandoff`/`forceLbs`, base shear, and all Design-tab stacking. The reaction off 208 plf + the level-2 wall reaction transferred down equals the old single 582-plf reaction by construction, so the on-plan point loads (11.35k in the user's case) and holdown stacking are byte-identical — only the line-load LABEL changed. So at `activeFloor===2` (roof) the plan still shows the roof diaphragm (374, parapets included) unchanged, and 1-story mode is untouched (`displayPlf` null). Engine guard not run this session at the user's request (display-only change, no guarded fn touched); esbuild compile clean. `APP_BUILD = 114` ("Version 1.14"). See §4ii.

> **rev 32 — UNIFIED MARKUP SCALE (reworks rev 30 + rev 31 at user's request).** The user decided the rev-30 text scaler and the rev-31 arrow/node halving should be ONE control: a single dropdown that scales text labels + load/reaction arrows + nodes together, with the base sizes back to original. So: **(a) reverted rev 31** — node dot/halo/stroke, `Reaction` shaft/stroke, and `WindLoad` standoff/tip/strokes are restored to their pre-rev-31 (original) literals; **(b) made the geometry scale** by the same factor that already scaled the text. Mechanics: the existing per-component `ts` prop (and the in-scope `markScale` for nodes) is now multiplied into the GEOMETRY too, not just font size — `Reaction` shaft `2.1·S·ts` + stroke `0.42·S·ts` (+ label gap `1.55·S·ts` so the whole rocket stays proportional); `WindLoad` `aLen …·0.5·S·ts`, tip `0.3·S·ts`, baseline `0.2·S·ts`, arrow `0.16·S·ts` (+ label gap `2.2·S·ts`); nodes dot `(isSel?1.05:0.85)·S·markScale`, halo `1.8·S·markScale`, stroke `0.25·S·markScale`, **and the draw-mode ghost-node preview `0.8·S·markScale`** so the preview matches a placed node. **Kept unscaled on purpose:** the node click/grab hit-target (`3.5·S`) so small nodes stay easy to hit; the `WindLoad` arrow COUNT/spacing (`n`, `5.5·S` — size scales, not density); the snap ring (an osnap affordance, not a node). **Arrowheads auto-scale** with their (now-scaled) stroke via the markers' default `markerUnits="strokeWidth"` — no marker edits. **Renames:** ribbon group **"Text" → "Markup"**, options bare `1×`/`0.75×`/`0.5×`/`0.25×`, tooltip rewritten; state **`textScale` → `markScale`** (`setMarkScale`), persisted under `markScale` with `else if("textScale" in s)` back-compat for any rev-30 `.wps`. **At `1×` the plan is byte-equivalent to rev 30's geometry** (original sizes); only `<1×` changes anything. **Engine guard CLEAN** (all 10 fns identical). Verification: compile, SSR render smoke (group reads "Markup", bare options, default `1×` selected), and a focused export test — `Reaction`/`WindLoad` strokes restored to originals at `ts=1` (4.2 / 2 / 1.6) and exactly halved at `ts=0.5`, shaft length 21→10.5, **arrow count invariant under scale**. Current build: `APP_BUILD = 113` ("Version 1.13").

> **rev 31 — PLAN GLYPHS HALVED (user-requested).** The user asked to halve three on-plan drawing elements (separate from rev 30's text scaling). All three are sized off `S` (`= max(view.w,view.h)/110`), so each is a literal-multiplier halving — no new state, no control (a definite one-time resize). **(1) Wall nodes** (`graph.nodes.map`): visible dot `(isSel?1.05:0.85)·S → (isSel?0.525:0.425)·S`, selection halo `1.8·S → 0.9·S`, stroke `0.25·S → 0.125·S`; **the transparent hit-target stays `3.5·S`** so nodes remain easy to click/grab. **(2) Point-load (reaction) arrow** (`Reaction`): shaft `2.1·S → 1.05·S`, stroke `0.42·S → 0.21·S`. **(3) plf line-load arrows** (`WindLoad`): standoff `aLen = clamp(…)·0.5·S → ·0.25·S`, tip `0.3·S → 0.15·S`, baseline stroke `0.2·S → 0.1·S`, arrow stroke `0.16·S → 0.08·S`. **Both arrowheads auto-halve**: the `#reactArr`/`#loadArr` markers have no `markerUnits`, so they default to `strokeWidth` and scale with the (now-halved) stroke — no marker edits needed. Untouched on purpose: the `WindLoad` arrow COUNT (`n`, spacing `5.5·S`) and label-offset constants (labels are text, handled by rev-30 `textScale`); the draw-mode ghost node / snap ring (transient drawing aids, not "the nodes"). **Engine guard CLEAN** — all 10 engine/stacking fns byte-identical; the diff is exactly the 7 visual lines + the `APP_BUILD` bump. Verification: esbuild compile, SSR render smoke, and a focused export test confirming the halved stroke widths render (`Reaction` 4.2→2.1, `WindLoad` baseline 2→1 / arrows 1.6→0.8) and the old values are gone. Current build: `APP_BUILD = 112` ("Version 1.12").

> **rev 30 — TEXT SCALE control on the Plan Sketcher toolbar (user-requested).** On a large plan zoomed out, the on-plan labels stay a roughly constant *screen* size (their fontSize is `1.35·S`, and `S = max(view.w,view.h)/110` grows as you zoom out), so the text ends up blanketing the small drawing. Fix: a **View ▸ Text** `<select>` (`1×`/`0.75×`/`0.5×`/`0.25×`, default `1×`) drives a new `textScale` state that multiplies the font size of every on-plan label. **Surface (all sketcher-canvas text, nothing in the wind-window modal or section diagrams):** `Tag` (dimension boxes + the reaction-rocket chip — font AND box scale together so the chip shrinks, not just its glyphs), `WindLoad` (the `… plf` label), `Reaction` (its `Tag`), plus the two inline canvas texts — the draw-mode live length (`{L}′`) and the `⚠ imbalance` flag. Each got a `ts=1` prop / `*textScale` factor; **`ts` defaults to 1, so every pre-existing call site and the SSR smokes render byte-identically to rev 29.** Drawing geometry (arrows, strokes, nodes, boxes' *positions*) is untouched — only text size (and the `Tag` box that wraps text) responds. **Persistence:** `textScale` rides in the sketcher `.wps` session (`get()` adds it; `set()` restores via `if("textScale" in s)` → old files default to `1`). This is sketcher session-UI, NOT part of `loadProject`'s `ui`/`design`/`calc` schema, so the schema tripwire is unaffected. **Engine guard CLEAN** — `calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `lineReactions`, `buildSecData`, `findLeewardPartner`, `lineResults`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults`, `upliftStk`, `withUtil` all byte-identical (verified by extract-and-diff). Verification: esbuild compile, comment-lexer clean, SSR render smoke (Text group + all four options + View/Stories intact), and a focused component test (Tag fontSize 13.5→6.75 at ts .5, box width shrinks, omitted-`ts`≡1, Reaction 3.375 at ts .25). Current build: `APP_BUILD = 111` ("Version 1.11").

> **rev 29 — DEPLOYED TO VERCEL (Vite host scaffold; NO app-code change).** The app is now a deployed static site (GitHub web UI → Vercel auto-deploy). To make the single-file React component buildable by Vite, a thin host shell was added AROUND it — the app jsx itself is byte-identical (engine + the 7 guarded fns untouched, `APP_BUILD` still 110 = "Version 1.10"). **Files (the deployable repo, see §4dd for full contents):** `index.html` (Vite entry — mounts `#root`, loads `./main.jsx`, plus a 4-line `html,body{margin:0}` host reset because the app's roots size to `calc(100vh − 46px)` and it never resets default body margin → avoids a gutter; the reset lives in the SHELL, not the app file) · `main.jsx` (imports `react` + `react-dom/client`, imports `App` from `./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, mounts under `React.StrictMode`) · `package.json` (deps `react`/`react-dom` ^18.3.1, dev `vite` ^5.4.10 + `@vitejs/plugin-react` ^4.3.4, version "1.10.0", scripts dev/build/preview) · `vite.config.js` (just the React plugin) · `.gitignore` (node_modules, dist, .vercel, …). **Why this is all it needs:** the only real `import` in the app is `react` (the `…xlsx` hits are inside comments); no CSS-file imports (all styling is injected `<style>` strings; IBM Plex loads from Google Fonts at runtime); no `import.meta` / `process.env`; no `ReactDOM` inside the app file — so the shell just has to mount it. **No `vercel.json` is required** — the app navigates via internal tab state (no react-router / URL routes), so there's nothing to rewrite. **Vercel settings:** auto-detected Vite — Build `npm run build`, Output `dist`, Install `npm install` (no overrides). **⚠ Actual repo layout is FLAT** (all files at repo root; `index.html` loads `./main.jsx`; `main.jsx` imports `./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`) — note the rev-29 chat *prose* sketched a `src/`-nested layout, but the delivered zip is flat and is the source of truth. **Handoff sync gap closed:** this rev also adds the previously-missing step of committing THIS handoff MD into the repo alongside the code (it had been left out of the first push). **STILL OPEN — the one live sign-off:** preview the stacked 1st-floor detailing + a two-story `.wps` save/open on the live Vercel URL to close out the Step-7 two-story feature. Current build: `APP_BUILD = 110` ("Version 1.10").

> **rev 28 — TWO-STORY: STEP 7a/7c — SECONDARY DETAILING WIRED TO THE STACKED DEMAND + REGRESSION LOCK (landed).** Step 6 stacked end post + uplift + holdown; rev 28 extends the same arm-aware stacking to the rest of the 1st-floor detailing: **anchor (`anchorSel`/`anchorEnd`), embedment (`embed`/`embedEnd`), straps (`altStrap`/`strapCorner`, via a stacked `upStrap_*`/`maxStrap` at the E56/E57 denominator of 3″), deflection (`deflW`/`deflS`) and footing (`reqFtgLen`/`LminS`/`LminW`)** now all derive from the stacked moment/uplift. Done by mirroring `calcSegment`'s own `anchorFor`/`embedFor`/`strapFor`/`defl`/footing-quad formula shapes inside `stackSeg` — **the 7 guarded engine fns stay byte-identical (guard CLEAN).** `stackSeg`'s signature became `(r1, r2, L, g, d, h)` so it has the species/grade/anchor/footing/height it needs; `stackedLineResults` passes `line1.heightFt` as `h`. **Deflection note:** the shear `v` is unchanged (the 1st-floor story shear was already carried by Step 5's combined load); only the chord/bending term uses the STACKED (≥) end post, so a stacked wall with a bigger required chord reports a *smaller* 1st-floor inter-story Δ — the as-built behavior (flagged in the UI note). **Footing** uses the stacked moments/uplifts with the 1st-floor's own dead load + base shear (`r1.B`/`r1.BwDL`/`r1.CwDL`/`r1.Fs`/`r1.Fw`), the same dead-load convention Step 6 set. The Design-tab note was rewritten — it no longer says anchor/strap/deflection/footing are unstacked; it now states every row reflects the stacked demand and explains the Δ behavior. **Calc-sheet interaction (unchanged, by design):** "Send line to calculation sheet" (`applyToCalc`) still sends only geometry + selType + `forceLbs`; the Calculation tab remains a single-line/single-floor view and does NOT apply moment stacking — stacking lives only in the Design tab's `resultsByLine`. Regression: new checked-in `work/test_stacking_step7.cjs` (25 asserts: §4aa 160 k·ft/16,203-lb example; exact discrete buckets HDU5→SSTB24→Simpson + STHD14/None strap on a 5000-lb stacked uplift; end-to-end via `stackedLineResults` with real engine floors + monotonic relations stacked-vs-single + top-floor-no-stack). **Step 7b (landed, same rev):** a frozen v2 two-story fixture (`work/fixtures/fixture_v2_2story.wps`), a 31-assert round-trip test (`work/test_loadstate_2story.cjs`) proving `H2`/`linesByFloor`/`ui.twoStory`/`ui.activeFloor` survive the pure `loadProject`/`mergeWallProps` core (+ v1 back-compat, newer-version, and stale-line paths), and a schema tripwire (`work/test_schema.cjs` + `work/fixtures/schema.expected.json`) that fires on any rename/add/remove of a schema-bearing default field — verified to trip on a simulated `H2`→`h2` rename. 7b is test/fixture infrastructure only; persistence already worked, so the jsx is unchanged. **Step 7 is COMPLETE** (the two-story feature, Steps 1–7, is feature-complete pending live sign-off). Current build: `APP_BUILD = 110` ("Version 1.10").

> **rev 27 — TWO-STORY: STEP 6 ARM-AWARE VERTICAL LOAD STACKING (landed).** The 1st-floor shear walls now carry the upper story's overturning with the correct moment arm. Because Step 5 already handed each floor the right force AND design height, the arm-aware base moment is exactly the SUM of the two floors' engine overturning moments for the same vertically-aligned segment: **M_base = Mot(1st) + Mot(2nd)** (e.g. roof 5k @ 20ft + 2nd-floor 6k @ 10ft over a 10ft wall → (5·20+6·10)/10 = **16k**, NOT a flat 11k). End post + holdown (+ a new "Overturning M · stacked" row and an explanatory note) are re-derived from that combined moment in a post-process wrapper (`stackedLineResults`/`stackSeg`/`upliftStk`) that mirrors the engine's own formula shapes — **`calcSegment`/`lineResults` and all 7 guarded fns stay byte-identical** (the new helpers are separate functions; engine guard CLEAN). Shear/nailing are unaffected (the combined shear was already carried by Step 5's 534-level load). Only the 1st floor in 2-story mode stacks; the 2nd floor and 1-story mode use plain `lineResults`, unchanged. Scope note (flagged in the UI + below): anchor / strap / deflection / footing rows still show the single-floor 1st-story demand — wiring those to the stacked uplift folds into Step 7. PENDING · Step 7 persistence/regression/finalize. Current build: `APP_BUILD = 109` ("Version 1.09").

> **rev 26 — TWO-STORY WOOD SHEAR WALL DESIGN (Steps 1–5).** Adding a simple two-story option (the building's two floors share one footprint + shear-wall layout, so they stay identical and vertically aligned; the upper story's load transfers down). Engine (`calcSegment` + the 7 guarded fns) stays byte-identical throughout — all new structural logic lives OUTSIDE the engine. Built step-by-step with the user testing each in the live preview before the next. Landed (see **§4z**): Step 1 (build 101–102) 1-Story/2-Story sliding pill + below-canvas floor selector · Step 2 (build 103) per-wall 2nd-story height `H2` data model · Step 3 (build 104) the two diaphragm line-load formulas (roof + 2nd-floor) shown live in the wind window · Step 4 (build 105–106) two-story section-cut elevation (`SecDiagram2`) with both diaphragm callouts + full windward/leeward height parity · Step 5 (builds 107–108) on-plan loads floor-aware (`propsForActive`) + BOTH floors designed and switchable in the Design tab (`designLinesByFloor` + a greyed-until-2-story floor switcher; shared `segsByLine`).

## 0. START HERE — how to resume this project (read me first)

**This project = the app + the engine module + this handoff + the engine guards + the deploy scaffold:** `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` (the app) · `calcCore.js` (the shear-wall engine module, rev-33 split — §4hh) · this handoff · `test_str1_golden.mjs` + `test_str1_design.mjs` (engine guards) · the rev-29 Vite host shell (`index.html` · `main.jsx` · `package.json` · `vite.config.js` · `.gitignore`, see §4dd) that makes it deployable · and separately `STRUCTURAL_SUITE_UI_THEME.md` (a *different* task — see bottom). **The whole repo (app + engine module + scaffold + this handoff) is what's committed to GitHub → Vercel; `src/` now holds `main.jsx`, `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, AND `calcCore.js`.**

**Standing rules for every session (do these automatically, without being asked):**
- **Preview on resume.** As soon as you've read this handoff, preview the current `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` in chat — copy it to `/mnt/user-data/outputs/` and present it so it renders as a live artifact — *before* writing the state summary and waiting for a task. The user wants to see the live app at the start of every session.
- **Run the test harness ONCE per chat, at the start.** After the preview, set up the harness (§6b) and run it a single time at the **beginning of the session** on the current code to establish a clean baseline (build + comment-lexer + render smoke + the engine byte-identity guard + whatever targeted suites exist). **Do NOT re-run the full sweep after every individual edit** — that burns tokens. Per change, the minimal guard is: esbuild compile, the engine byte-identity check (cheap, pure-Python), and a focused render/headless smoke for the *specific* thing you touched. Snapshot the engine baseline (`cp work/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx work/.engine-baseline.jsx`) as part of that one session-start run, before your first edit.
- **Handoff tracks code.** Any time the app is updated, update this MD in the **same session/response** as the code. That means: bump the rev line at the very top, add a new `§4*`-style rev subsection describing the change (additive/invariant tone, like the existing ones), update the rev number inside the §0 resume prompt, and adjust "Where rev N left off" / "Open items". Never hand back updated code with a stale handoff — the two always ship together.
- **Version bump.** On every app update, increment `APP_BUILD` by 1 at the top of the jsx (rev 25 introduced it at 100 = "Version 1.00", shown in the top bar). It rolls 199→"2.00" by construction. This is the user-facing version ONLY — never touch `CURRENT_VERSION` (save-file schema) to bump the display.

**Save-file status (as of rev 29):** the app is now **deployed to Vercel (rev 29)**, but the Save/Open (`.wps`) feature **has not been used in anger yet** — so **no real save files exist in the wild that could break.** The rev 23–24 forward-compat work and the save-file regression guards are therefore *pre-emptive insurance*, not protecting live data. Practical consequence: when adding fields, you still want the merge-on-defaults discipline so a future save round-trips, but you do **not** need to treat "an old `.wps` won't load" as a live-fire risk yet. (This stops being true the moment someone saves a real `.wps` from the live site — once the two-story sign-off below happens, assume real files may start to exist.)

**To keep building:**
1. **Push the latest code to GitHub** (web UI → Vercel auto-deploys) so your live app matches this file's rev. The repo holds the app + the rev-29 Vite scaffold (§4dd) + THIS handoff — commit all three together (the handoff was missing from the first push; rev 29 closes that gap). Every push to `main` auto-redeploys on Vercel.

**Where rev 60 left off (SEISMIC — 2-STORY MODULE: per-diaphragm weight + vertical distribution):** the seismic module now handles 2-story buildings. `seismicWeight2Story(graph, loop, twoStoryLoop, propsFor, isOne, roofDL, floorDL, wallDL)` splits the tributary wall weight — roof (L2) trib `par + H₂/2` over the 2-story walls only, floor (L1) trib `H₂/2 + H₁/2` (2-story) or `par + H₁/2` (1-story-tagged, C/D); area DL by level (floorDL+roofDL under the 2-story footprint via `twoStoryLoop.area`, roofDL over any 1-story-only footprint); `h_floor=H₁`, `h_roof=H₁+H₂`. `seismicDistribute2Story(sw2,Cs)` → `V`, `F_roof`, `F_floor` (`F=V·(W·h)/Σ(W·h)`). The plan distribution uses the ACTIVE-floor force on the right graph (roof → `twoStoryGraph`, floor → full), `w=F/(diaphragm bbox ⟂ force)` via the generalized `buildSecData`+`lineReactions`. The 2-Story Seismic Weight card shows per-level W/V/F + per-level plan plf; `wTotal` lift covers 2-story. VIEW-ONLY. `calcCore.js` + 8 app-file guarded fns BYTE-IDENTICAL. **Phase-5 EXACT** (W_total 243,990 / V 12,199.5 / F_roof 5,985 / F_floor 6,214 / plf 153.46·99.75 roof + 159.35·103.58 floor); `work/_test_seis2.cjs` 17/17, `work/_test_pipeline.cjs` 14/14 (conservation), `work/_test_mixed.cjs` 5/5 (C/D); compile + guard CLEAN; SSR mount PASS wind (36,899) + 2story-seismic (43,951). `APP_BUILD = 139`. **Deploy: replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js` UNCHANGED.** Preview: 2-Story pill, draw 60×39, set H 13/H₂ 10/par 6 + Roof 20/Floor 50/Wall 18/Cs 0.05 → Seismic Weight card reads W_total 243,990, V 12,199.5, F_roof 5,985/F_floor 6,214; flip **Load case → Seismic** and toggle the floor selector — Level 2 draws the roof plf (153.46/99.75), Level 1 the floor plf (159.35/103.58) with reactions. **Next:** wire the seismic reactions into the Design-tab seismic demand (envelope wind vs seismic per line); refine the mixed-height roof-area fallback for an open (non-closing) 2-story region.
