- **Schema tripwire.** `work/test_schema.cjs` + `work/fixtures/schema.expected.json` (**15 asserts**) re-derive the live key-sets of `DEF_SECTION`/`DEFAULT_G`/`DEFAULT_D`/`SEG_DEFAULTS`/`DEFAULT_LINE`/`DEFAULT_PLACED` and the `loadProject` output `ui`/`design`/`calc` shapes, compare to the frozen expected, and FAIL on any add/remove/rename — plus hardcoded presence checks for `H2`/`twoStory`/`activeFloor`/`linesByFloor` that survive a careless expected-file regen. **Verified to fire** on a simulated `H2`→`h2` rename (negative control). This is the guard that forces a future rename to ship with a `CURRENT_VERSION` bump + a `MIGRATIONS` step + a fixture — merge-on-defaults silently mis-loads renamed fields, so without this they'd pass unnoticed. **Caveat (unchanged from §4x):** line GEOMETRY-field renames (`id`/`a`/`b`/`lengthFt` — not in a default object) are NOT auto-caught; they rely on discipline.
- **Save-file status:** still no real `.wps` files in the wild (Save-Open hasn't been used in anger — the app is deployed as of rev 29, but no real save has been made yet), so 7b is pre-emptive insurance. If a breaking schema change ever lands, freeze a fixture at the OLD version and add a load-assertion (the migration checklist in §4x / §7). **New checked-in artifacts:** `work/exp.cjs`, `work/fixtures/fixture_v2_2story.wps`, `work/fixtures/schema.expected.json`, `work/test_loadstate_2story.cjs`, `work/test_schema.cjs` (+ the rev-28a `work/sw_stack.cjs`, `work/test_stacking_step7.cjs`). No app change; `APP_BUILD = 110`.






## 4dd. Rev 29 — Deployed to Vercel (Vite host scaffold; NO app-code change)

The app went live on Vercel. The single-file React component is byte-identical — a thin Vite host shell was added AROUND it so a static build can mount it. **`APP_BUILD` stays 110 ("Version 1.10"); engine + the 7 guarded fns untouched; the jsx was not edited.** This is an infrastructure rev, so there is no version bump (the version display tracks app-code changes, and there were none).

- **The deployable repo (FLAT layout — all files at root).** The delivered zip is the source of truth:
  ```
  (repo root)
  ├─ index.html                 ← Vite entry
  ├─ main.jsx                   ← mounts <App/>
  ├─ plan-sketcher-suite.jsx    ← the app, UNCHANGED
  ├─ package.json
  ├─ vite.config.js
  ├─ .gitignore
  └─ PLAN_SKETCHER_SUITE_HANDOFF.md   ← this file (added rev 29)
  ```
  **⚠ Layout note:** the rev-29 chat *prose* described a `src/`-nested layout (`src/main.jsx`, `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`). The actual delivered files are FLAT — `index.html` loads `./main.jsx`, and `main.jsx` imports `./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, both root-relative. If you re-issue the scaffold, match the flat layout that's live (or move both into `src/` AND update the two relative import paths together — don't half-do it).
- **`index.html`** — `#root` div + `<script type="module" src="./main.jsx">`. Carries a **4-line host reset**: `html,body{margin:0;padding:0}` + `#root{min-height:100vh}`. Reason: the app injects all its own styling but never resets the default body margin, and its roots size to `calc(100vh − 46px)` — without the reset you get a gutter. **This reset lives in the SHELL, not in the app file** (keeps the app byte-identical and portable).
- **`main.jsx`** — `import React from "react"` + `import ReactDOM from "react-dom/client"` + `import App from "./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx"`; `createRoot(#root).render(<React.StrictMode><App/></React.StrictMode>)`. The app's `export default function App()` is exactly what this expects.
- **`package.json`** — `"version":"1.10.0"`, `"type":"module"`; deps `react`/`react-dom` `^18.3.1`; devDeps `vite ^5.4.10` + `@vitejs/plugin-react ^4.3.4`; scripts `dev`/`build`/`preview`.
- **`vite.config.js`** — just `react()` plugin.
- **`.gitignore`** — `node_modules`, `dist`, `dist-ssr`, `.DS_Store`, `*.local`, `.vercel`, `npm-debug.log*`.
- **Why a bare mount suffices (re-verified against the source).** The only real `import` is `react` (the `…xlsx` grep hits are all inside comments, lines ~1962/1968/1969). No CSS-file imports (styling = injected `<style>` strings; IBM Plex from Google Fonts at runtime). No `import.meta`, no `process.env`, no `ReactDOM` inside the app file. So the shell's whole job is: provide React + react-dom and mount `<App/>`.
- **No `vercel.json`.** Navigation is internal tab state (no react-router / no URL routes) → nothing to rewrite, no SPA-fallback rule needed.
- **Vercel project settings (auto-detected Vite, no overrides):** Framework Preset **Vite** · Build `npm run build` · Output `dist` · Install `npm install`. Every push to `main` auto-redeploys.
- **Handoff-in-repo:** the first push omitted this MD; rev 29 adds it to the repo so the handoff travels with the code (per the §0 "handoff tracks code" rule, now also "handoff ships in the repo").
- **OPEN — the one live sign-off (unchanged target, now actionable on the live URL):** preview the stacked 1st-floor detailing and a two-story `.wps` save/open on the deployed Vercel site, then sign off to close the Step-7 two-story feature.

## 4ee. Rev 30 — Text Scale control on the Plan Sketcher toolbar (user-requested)

**The problem.** On-plan label text is sized `fontSize = 1.35·S`, where `S = Math.max(view.w, view.h)/110` (line ~1004). `S` grows as you zoom out (the viewBox widens), which keeps the label at a roughly **constant screen size** at any zoom. Great for a normal plan; bad for a large plan zoomed way out — the building shrinks but the labels don't, so they blanket the drawing. The user asked for a scaler to shrink them.

**The control.** A new ribbon group **Text** (a `<div className="rgroup">` with `rlabel` "Text"), placed **between View and Stories**, holding a single `<select className="rsel">` with options `1×` / `0.75×` / `0.5×` / `0.25×` (default `1×`). `value={textScale} onChange={e=>setTextScale(parseFloat(e.target.value))}` — state stays numeric so the components can multiply by it directly. New CSS class `.rsel` (added right after `.rbtn:disabled`) mirrors `.rbtn`'s look (white, ink, hover→accent, focus ring); it is a native select so it's keyboard/AX-friendly and needs no popover code.

**State.** `const [textScale,setTextScale]=useState(1);` declared in `PlanSketcher` immediately after `dims` (line ~911). Default `1` ⇒ no behavioral change from rev 29.

**Where it applies (the COMPLETE set of sketcher-canvas text — nothing in the wind-window modal / `SecDiagram*`, which are fixed-size in their own panel):**
- `Tag({…, ts=1})` — used by **dimension labels** and the **reaction rocket chip**. Scales `fs=1.35·S·ts` AND the box (`w` padding term, `h` via fs, `rx`, the text y-nudge) so the whole chip shrinks, not just the glyphs (a shrunk glyph in a full-size box wouldn't reduce obstruction).
- `WindLoad({…, ts=1})` — the `… plf` label (`fontSize={1.35*S*ts}`). Arrows/lines/offsets unchanged.
- `Reaction({…, ts=1})` — threads `ts` straight into its `<Tag … ts={ts}/>`.
- Two inline canvas texts in `PlanSketcher`: the **draw-mode live length** `{L}′` and the **`⚠ imbalance`** flag — each multiplied by `*textScale`.
- Mount sites pass `ts={textScale}`: `<WindLoad …>` (×2, h/v), `<Reaction …>` (×2), and the dimension `<Tag …>`.

**`ts` defaults to 1 on every component**, so all pre-existing call sites (and the SSR smokes, and any future re-use) render byte-identically. Only text size + the `Tag` box that wraps text respond to the control; **no drawing geometry** (strokes, arrows, nodes, grid, divides, box *positions*) moves.

**Persistence.** `textScale` is added to the sketcher session `get()` snapshot (`…, dims, textScale }`) and restored in `set()` via `if("textScale" in s) setTextScale(Number(s.textScale)||1);` — forward-compatible (old `.wps` lacking the field default to `1`). **This is sketcher session-UI, not part of `loadProject`'s `ui`/`design`/`calc` shapes, so the schema tripwire (`test_schema.cjs`) is unaffected** — no `schema.expected.json` regen needed.

**Engine guard CLEAN.** All app-code changes are in: the `APP_BUILD` const, the `CSS` template (`.rsel`), the three module-scope sketcher visuals (`Tag`/`WindLoad`/`Reaction`), and `PlanSketcher` (state + ribbon JSX + two inline texts + session get/set). The engine and the 10 engine/stacking functions verified this rev (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `lineReactions`, `buildSecData`, `findLeewardPartner`, `lineResults`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults`, `upliftStk`, `withUtil` — a superset of the canonical "7 guarded fns") are byte-identical — verified by extract-and-diff against `.engine-baseline.jsx` (all 10 IDENTICAL).

**Verification.** esbuild compile OK; comment-lexer clean; SSR render smoke (asserts the **Text** group, all four options, default value 1, and that the **View** Fit button + **Stories** pill survive); focused component test exporting `Tag`/`Reaction`: `Tag` fontSize `13.5→6.75` at `ts .5`, box `width` shrinks, **omitted-`ts` ≡ `ts:1`**, `Reaction` label `3.375` at `ts .25`. Render length 30,940 → 31,769 (the added dropdown). Build `APP_BUILD = 111` ("Version 1.11").

**Judgment call (reversible).** The draw-mode **live length** readout also obeys `textScale`, so at `0.25×` it gets small while drawing. Included for consistency (it's on-plan text like the rest); exempting it is a one-line change (drop `*textScale` on that single inline `<text>`) if the user prefers it always full-size.

## 4ff. Rev 31 — Plan glyphs halved: nodes, point-load arrow, plf line-load arrows (user-requested)

The user asked to halve three on-plan drawing elements (distinct from rev 30, which scaled *text*; this scales *glyphs/geometry*). All three derive their size from `S = Math.max(view.w,view.h)/110`, so each change is a literal-multiplier halving with a `rev 31:` inline comment for find/revert. **No state, no control** — the user asked for a definite "half the size," not an adjustable knob.

- **(1) Wall nodes** — the `graph.nodes.map(p=>…)` block in `PlanSketcher`:
  - visible dot `r={(isSel?1.05:0.85)*S}` → `r={(isSel?0.525:0.425)*S}`
  - selection halo `r={1.8*S}` → `r={0.9*S}` (kept proportional to the smaller dot)
  - dot stroke `strokeWidth={0.25*S}` → `{0.125*S}`
  - **the transparent hit-target `r={3.5*S}` is intentionally NOT halved** — it's the click/right-click/grab target; shrinking it would hurt usability. (A comment marks it.)
- **(2) Point-load (reaction) arrow** — `Reaction` (module scope):
  - `shaft = 2.1*S` → `1.05*S`
  - line `strokeWidth={0.42*S}` → `{0.21*S}`
  - the `#reactArr` arrowhead **auto-halves**: the marker has no `markerUnits`, so it defaults to `strokeWidth` and scales with the halved stroke. The kips label (`<Tag>`) is text — untouched here (sized by rev-30 `ts`); with the shorter shaft it simply sits closer to the node.
- **(3) plf line-load arrows** — `WindLoad` (module scope):
  - standoff/length `aLen = clamp(total/55,3,8)*0.5*S` → `*0.25*S`
  - `tip = 0.3*S` → `0.15*S` (so the drawn arrow shaft, `aLen−tip`, also halves)
  - baseline `strokeWidth={0.2*S}` → `{0.1*S}`; arrow `strokeWidth={0.16*S}` → `{0.08*S}` (the `#loadArr` arrowhead auto-halves with the stroke)
  - **untouched on purpose:** the arrow COUNT `n = max(2, round(len/(5.5*S)))` (density, not size — the user wanted smaller arrows, not fewer) and the `… plf` label offset `aLen+2.2*S` (text; it follows the smaller `aLen` inward, which is fine).

**Not touched (scope discipline):** the draw-mode ghost node (`r={0.8*S}`) and the node-snap ring (`r={1.5*S}`) are transient drawing aids, not "the nodes," so they were left as-is. If the user notices the draw-preview dot looks bigger than the placed node, halving that one `0.8*S` is a trivial follow-up.

**Engine guard CLEAN.** The whole diff vs `.engine-baseline.jsx` is the `APP_BUILD` bump + exactly 7 visual lines (3 node, 2 `Reaction`, 4 `WindLoad` constants across 2 lines for stroke/aLen/tip). All 10 engine/stacking fns extract-and-diff IDENTICAL. **Verification:** esbuild compile OK; SSR render smoke (App mounts, nodes present); focused export test of `Reaction`/`WindLoad` confirms the halved stroke widths render (`Reaction` 4.2→2.1; `WindLoad` baseline 2→1, arrows 1.6→0.8) and the pre-halve values are gone. Build `APP_BUILD = 112` ("Version 1.12").

**If the user wants a different size later:** the knobs are the seven `rev 31:`-commented lines. Promoting them to one module-level constant (e.g. `const PLAN_GLYPH = 0.5;` multiplied into each) — or a toolbar control mirroring the rev-30 Text dropdown — is the natural next step *if and only if* they ask for adjustability; until then, literals keep it simple.

> **SUPERSEDED by rev 32 (§4gg):** the user chose exactly that "toolbar control" path — rev 32 reverted this hard-halving and folded nodes + arrows into the rev-30 dropdown as one unified scale. §4ff is retained as change-log history; the live behavior is in §4gg.

## 4gg. Rev 32 — Unified "Markup" scale: text + arrows + nodes on one dropdown (user-requested)

**The decision.** After rev 31, the user said the arrows/nodes should be **scalable together with the text**, at original base size — i.e. merge rev 30 (text scaler) and rev 31 (arrow/node size) into ONE control. So rev 32 reverts rev 31's hardcoded halving and makes the single dropdown scale the whole on-plan markup layer.

- **Revert + scale (base literals restored, then × the scale factor):**
  - **Nodes** (`graph.nodes.map`, `markScale` in scope): dot `(isSel?1.05:0.85)*S*markScale`, halo `1.8*S*markScale`, stroke `0.25*S*markScale`. The transparent **hit-target stays `3.5*S` (unscaled)** so a node shrunk to `0.25×` is still easy to click/grab. Also the **draw-mode ghost-node preview** `0.8*S*markScale` (rev 31 had left it; now it tracks so the preview matches the placed node). Snap ring `1.5*S` left unscaled (osnap affordance).
  - **Reaction** (point-load arrow, prop `ts`): `shaft=2.1*S*ts`, stroke `0.42*S*ts`, label gap `1.55*S*ts` (so arrow + gap + label chip scale as one rocket).
  - **WindLoad** (plf arrows, prop `ts`): `aLen = clamp(…)*0.5*S*ts`, `tip=0.3*S*ts`, baseline stroke `0.2*S*ts`, arrow stroke `0.16*S*ts`, label gap `2.2*S*ts`. The arrow **COUNT** `n=max(2,round(len/(5.5*S)))` is deliberately NOT scaled — scale changes glyph size, not density.
  - Arrowheads (`#reactArr`, `#loadArr`) auto-scale with their now-scaled stroke (markers default to `markerUnits="strokeWidth"`).
- **`ts` is the scale factor.** `Reaction`/`WindLoad`/`Tag` already received `ts={markScale}` (rev 30, for text); rev 32 simply multiplies `ts` into their geometry as well. Default `ts=1` ⇒ original size, so any other caller / DesignPlan reuse is unaffected.
- **Renames (UI + state):**
  - Ribbon group label **"Text" → "Markup"**; options changed from `Text 1×`… to bare `1×` / `0.75×` / `0.5×` / `0.25×`; tooltip rewritten ("…shrink the labels, the load/reaction arrows, AND the nodes together…").
  - State **`textScale` → `markScale`** / `setMarkScale`. Persisted in the `.wps` sketcher session under `markScale`; restore reads `if("markScale" in s) … else if("textScale" in s) …` so any rev-30-era save still loads. (Still sketcher session-UI, not `loadProject` schema — tripwire unaffected.)
- **`1×` == original.** Because the base literals are the pre-rev-31 originals and the multiplier defaults to 1, a `1×` plan is byte-equivalent to rev 30's geometry; only `<1×` changes pixels.

**Engine guard CLEAN** — all 10 engine/stacking fns extract-and-diff IDENTICAL. The full diff is the `APP_BUILD` bump + the markup/scale lines only. **Verification:** esbuild compile OK; SSR render smoke (group reads "Markup", bare options, default `1×` selected, App mounts); focused export test — `Reaction`/`WindLoad` strokes restored to originals at `ts=1` (4.2 / baseline 2 / arrows 1.6) and exactly halved at `ts=0.5` (2.1 / 1 / 0.8), shaft length 21→10.5, and **arrow `<line>` count invariant across scales** (size, not density). Build `APP_BUILD = 113` ("Version 1.13").

**Tweaks if asked:** base sizes live in the `rev 32:`-commented lines (nodes block, `Reaction`, `WindLoad`); a smaller floor or different default is one `<option>` / the `useState(1)` initial; promoting the scale into a shared constant isn't needed since `markScale`/`ts` already is that single factor.

## 4hh. Rev 33 — Shear-wall engine extracted to `calcCore.js` (first file split; user-requested)

The user asked to start splitting the monolithic single-file app into modules (motivation: easier debugging + not re-uploading the whole 4k-line file for every change), beginning with the calc engine and doing the rest later. This rev extracts ONLY the shear-wall calculation engine into a new sibling module `src/calcCore.js`. It is a **pure text move — zero behavioral change** (proven two ways below). `APP_BUILD` stays **113 ("Version 1.13")**: like the rev-29 Vite scaffold, this is structural/infra, and the user-facing version tracks app-code behavior changes, of which there are none.

- **What moved (verbatim) into `src/calcCore.js`:** the data `SCHEDULE`, `SCHEDULE_STR1`, `schedFor`, `NAIL_EDGE`, `CODES`, `HD_TABLE`; the helpers `isNum`, `xMax`, `numOr0`, `CP`; and the engine fns `calcSegment`, `baseDesignSeg`, `evaluateCandidate`, `generateDesign`. These were lines ~1989–2198 of the rev-32 file (the whole block between the "PLYWOOD SHEAR WALL MODULE" banner and the `// ---------- Formatting + dark theme` comment). `calcCore.js` ends with one `export { … }` of all 14 names.
- **Why this block specifically (clean cut, no circular import):** the shear engine is **self-contained** — it references only `Math.*` and helpers defined within the block (`schedFor`/`xMax`/`CP`/`HD_TABLE`/`numOr0`/`isNum`). It does NOT use any geometry helper (`keyOf`/`clamp`/`dist`/…) or React. So it can live in its own module with **no imports back into the app file** → no circular dependency. (The wind engine `lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`findLeewardPartner` is NOT self-contained — it uses the geometry helpers that `PlanSketcher` also uses — which is exactly why it was left for a later split that also extracts `geometry.js`.)
- **What the app file imports back:** the 10 names actually referenced outside the block — `calcSegment, generateDesign, baseDesignSeg, schedFor, HD_TABLE, NAIL_EDGE, CODES, isNum, xMax, numOr0` — via `import { … } from "./calcCore.js";` placed immediately after the React import. (`CP`, `evaluateCandidate`, `SCHEDULE`, `SCHEDULE_STR1` have no external callers — they stay internal to `calcCore.js` but are still exported for the test harness / future modules.) The "PLYWOOD SHEAR WALL MODULE" banner comment stays in the app file with an added note that the engine now lives in `calcCore.js`.
- **Still in `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` (deliberately, for the later split):** the wind engine (`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`findLeewardPartner`), the design/stacking logic (`lineResults`/`stackSeg`/`stackedLineResults`/`upliftStk`/`withUtil`/`postAllowable`/`hdCapacity`), all React components, `fmt`, the themes/CSS, persistence (`loadProject`/`migrateProject`/`DEFAULT_*`), and `App`. `fmt` calls `isNum` (now imported) — fine.
- **Proven byte-identical TWO ways.** (1) **Engine guard:** all **12** guarded fns (`calcSegment`, `generateDesign`, `evaluateCandidate`, `baseDesignSeg`, `lineReactions`, `buildSecData`, `findLeewardPartner`, `lineResults`, `withUtil`, `stackSeg`, `stackedLineResults`, `upliftStk`) extract-and-diff **IDENTICAL** vs the rev-32 baseline — the 4 moved ones found in `calcCore.js`, the other 8 in the app file. (2) **Rendered-App diff:** bundled `App` from the rev-32 monolith AND from the post-split pair, `renderToString`'d both → **byte-for-byte identical, 32,000 chars each**. Plus: both files esbuild-compile (the `./calcCore.js` import resolves), comment-balance clean in both, and a direct functional test of `calcCore.js` as an imported module (all 14 exports present; the Structural-I golden `vW = 438.75`; `schedFor("str1")` caps 475/715/930; `schedFor(undefined) === SCHEDULE`).
- **Deploy (IMPORTANT — this push ADDS a file).** The repo `src/` now holds **three** source files: `main.jsx` (unchanged — still `import App from "./plan-sketcher-suite.jsx"`), `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` (replaced — engine block removed, import added), and **`calcCore.js` (NEW — must be created in the repo)**. `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js`, `.gitignore` are all unchanged (Vite resolves the new relative import automatically; no config needed). So via GitHub web UI: add `src/calcCore.js`, replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, and re-commit this handoff.
- **Preview workflow note (changed by the split).** A multi-file app no longer renders as a standalone Claude artifact (the artifact runtime can't resolve `./calcCore.js`). To keep the §0 "preview as a live artifact" rule working, **bundle `calcCore.js` + `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` into one temp single-file jsx and present THAT** (concatenate calcCore minus its `export`, then the app file minus its `calcCore` import — or esbuild-bundle). The committed repo stays modular; the preview is a throwaway bundle.
- **Harness impact (see §6/§6b updates):** the engine byte-identity guard now searches BOTH `calcCore.js` (moved fns) and the app file (the rest), and its extractor handles `const name =` arrows (e.g. `upliftStk`) as well as `function name(`. The golden-suite bundle step now bundles `calcCore.js` directly (it already exports the engine) instead of appending an `export` to a copy of the app file.
- **NEXT (the "rest later" the user deferred):** (a) `geometry.js` (`clamp`/`dist`/`keyOf`/`fmt1`/`fmt2`/`niceStep`/`wallAng`/`segInt`/`computeCut`/`buildFrom`/`loopInfo`/`pointInRing`/`mergeWallProps`/`DEF_SECTION`) + `windEngine.js` (`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`findLeewardPartner`) — these move together because the wind engine depends on the geometry helpers, which `PlanSketcher` ALSO imports; (b) `designLogic.js` (the stacking/`withUtil` block); (c) the big UI modules (`sketcher.jsx`, `calcSheet.jsx`, `designTab.jsx`) + `App.jsx`. Group by change-frequency to minimize multi-file web-UI commits. Each step: text-move only, keep the engine/render guards green, bundle a preview.

## 4ii. Rev 34 — Floor diaphragm stops double-counting the roof load (2-story display fix; user-requested)

The user (PE/SE) flagged a load-path error in the section-cut window: in 2-story mode the **2nd-floor diaphragm** line load was shown as `wallRes + wallRes2 + roofLL` — i.e. it added the *entire roof diaphragm* (incl. parapets) into the floor diaphragm (e.g. 104 + 104 + 374 = **582 plf**). That is physically wrong. The roof diaphragm does not pour into the floor diaphragm; it dumps into the **2nd-story shear wall**, which transfers down into the **1st-story shear wall as a point load**. The floor diaphragm itself spans only the half-walls directly above and below it. Correct floor diaphragm = `wallRes + wallRes2` = ½·H·pw + ½·H₂·pw = 104 + 104 = **208 plf**. This is a **display fix only** — the reactions/point loads and the stacked overturning/holdown were already correct and must not change.

- **Why the reactions don't move.** The 1st-floor on-plan reaction (11.35k in the user's 60×39 ft, H=H₂=13, pw=16 case) was computed from the COMBINED load via `propsForActive`'s `H_eff = H + 2·H₂` (582 plf). That single reaction equals the floor-only diaphragm reaction (208 plf → 4.06k) **plus** the level-2 shear-wall reaction transferred down (374 plf → 7.29k): 4.06 + 7.29 = 11.35k. So lumping it as 582→11.35k vs. stacking 208+roof-via-wall gives the identical total. The fix therefore changes ONLY the displayed line-load label; the combined-load path that produces the point loads is left exactly as-is.
- **`floorDiaphragmPlf` (new helper, next to `propsForActive`).** `useCallback(key => 0.5·(p.pw)·((p.H)+(p.H₂)))` using `propsFor(key)` (the REAL, un-substituted props). Note the leeward-parapet term and the windward parapet term BOTH cancel out of `combined − roof` (they live only in the roof diaphragm), so the floor diaphragm load is **uniform along a wall** — no per-region subdivision, hence one label.
- **`WindLoad` gains `displayPlf` (default null).** When non-null, it renders a SINGLE span `wa→wb` at `displayPlf` instead of the rev-18 per-region coalesced `subLoads`. The plan passes `displayPlf={twoStory && activeFloor===1 ? floorDiaphragmPlf(wl.key) : null}` for both `secH`/`secV` windward walls. So: 1st-floor 2-story view → floor-only label; 2nd-floor view (`displayPlf` null) → roof diaphragm label (374, parapets included) unchanged; 1-story mode (`displayPlf` null) → byte-identical to before.
- **Within-wall dashed divides hidden on the 1st floor.** The `secData.divides` render is gated with `!(twoStory && activeFloor===1)`. Those divides mark where the per-region (combined) plf changes along a wall — driven by leeward-parapet variation, which belongs to the ROOF diaphragm. With the floor load uniform, a divide would contradict the single 208 label, so it's suppressed on the 1st floor only (still drawn on the 2nd floor and in 1-story mode). [If the user prefers them kept, un-gate this one render.]
- **`WindWindow` section-cut panel.** `floorLL = wallRes + wallRes2` (dropped `+ roofLL`); the "roof load transferred ↓" breakdown `<div>` is removed (the two remaining rows — ½·H₂·pw lower-half + ½·H·pw upper-half — now sum to the displayed 208). `SecDiagram2` already takes `floorLL` only for the gold "2nd-flr diaphragm" callout text (the dashed diaphragm LINE is positioned from heights, not the load), so it updates automatically with no geometry change. `roofLL` is unchanged (374) — the roof diaphragm is correct as-is.
- **Untouched (verified by reading, not by guard this session — user asked not to run tests):** `buildSecData`, `lineReactions`, `findLeewardPartner` (all guarded), `propsForActive` (1st floor still `H_eff = H + 2·H₂`), `secH`/`secV`, `runDesignHandoff`/`forceLbs`, the status-bar base shear, and the entire Design tab + stacking. No guarded engine fn was edited. esbuild compiles both files clean (only the pre-existing duplicate-key warnings in the unused dark `Elevation`). `APP_BUILD = 114` ("Version 1.14").
- **Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY. `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` are all unchanged.

## 4jj. Rev 35 — Mixed-height two-story · Step 1/4: one-story wall tagging (user-requested, multi-step)

The user wants to model buildings that are two-story overall but where some walls/portions are only one story (single-story or open-to-above) — e.g. the 2-story box inside a 1-story perimeter in the attached schematics. We agreed a full behavior spec and a 4-step build (each step previewed by the user before the next, like the original two-story feature in §4z). A one-story wall = a diaphragm-connectivity statement: it feeds the **floor** diaphragm (its parapet + top-half + its own roof, which sits at the floor-diaphragm level) and the **foundation**, but never the **roof** diaphragm.

**Step 1 (this rev) is the tag + appearance ONLY — no load/analysis change.** With no walls tagged, the app is byte-identical to rev 34. Edits (all in `plan-sketcher-suite.jsx`, none in the guarded engine):
- **State** `const [oneStory,setOneStory]=useState(()=>new Set())` declared next to `noSupport`.
- **Helper** `isOneStory = useCallback(key => twoStory && oneStory.has(key))` next to `isSup`. **Toggle** `toggleOneStory(edge)` next to `toggleSupport`.
- **Menu** new wall-menu button `↧ Switch to 1-story / ↥ Switch to 2-story`, gated `{twoStory && (…)}`, between "Takes point load" and "Add node here".
- **Appearance** wall stroke uses `oneSty?C_ONESTORY:C_WALL` with new const `C_ONESTORY="#2E6B4F"` (the design-palette green). The non-load-bearing dashed/dimmed style is applied independently, so a wall that is both reads green + dashed + dimmed.
- **Split migration** `setOneStory(...)` mirrors the `noSupport` line in `splitWall` — both halves inherit the tag.
- **Persistence** `oneStory:[...oneStory]` added to the sketcher `get()`; `setOneStory(new Set(s.oneStory||[]))` in `set()` (old files → empty). This is sketcher SESSION-UI, NOT in `loadProject`'s schema, so the schema tripwire is unaffected (same as `noSupport`/`markScale`).
- **Warning** `allOneStory = useMemo(()=> twoStory && graph.edges.length>0 && graph.edges.every(e=>oneStory.has(keyOf(e))))`; renders an amber top-right overlay `⚠ All walls are 1-story — the 2nd floor has no walls` via new `.allonestory-warn` CSS (mirrors `.floorbadge`, sits top-right so it never collides with the top-left floor badge).
- **`APP_BUILD = 115`** ("Version 1.15").

**Engine guard CLEAN** — all 12 guarded fns (`findLeewardPartner`/`lineReactions`/`buildSecData`/`lineResults`/`stackSeg`/`stackedLineResults`/`upliftStk`/`withUtil` + `calcSegment`/`generateDesign`/`baseDesignSeg`/`evaluateCandidate`) extract-and-diff identical to the rev-34 baseline. esbuild compile clean (pre-existing dup-key warning in the unused dark `Elevation` only); SSR render smoke PASS (32,149 chars).

**Confirmed spec (locked before coding) — drives Steps 2–4:**
- **Step 2 — 2nd-floor (roof) exclusion.** On the 2nd-floor view only two-story walls exist. Implement by handing `buildSecData` a FILTERED graph = the full graph minus one-story walls (+ their orphaned nodes) and a recomputed `loop`; the full graph still RENDERS all walls (green ones drawn, load-less). This drops 1-story walls from windward collection, the `overlapShadow` test, AND `lineReactions` supports in one move — engine untouched. (NB: zeroing via `propsFor` is NOT enough — a 1-story wall geometrically in front of the box would wrongly *shadow* the box; removing it from the graph is the fix.)
- **Step 3 — 1st-floor accumulation (the 454).** A windward wall's floor-diaphragm plf VARIES along its length: at each across-wind station it sums the connected strips in its downwind shadow — its own ½·H·pw (+ its parapet if it is 1-story, whose roof is at the floor level) + the **bottom half of any two-story wall behind it (½·H₂·pw, one face)** + leeward parapet. So the front wall splits into regions (e.g. 454 where the box is behind it, 374 where it isn't). The app ALREADY walks back-walls + subdivides the windward span for the leeward parapet (`backs`/breakpoints/`subLoads` in `buildSecData`); Step 3 is a NEW wind fn that extends that pattern to also add the back two-story wall's ½·H₂, then reuses `lineReactions` for the point loads — guarded `buildSecData` stays byte-identical. Worked example from the user's schematic: `32×5 + 16×13/2 + 22×5 (=374, the front 1-story wall) + 16×10/2 (=80, the box behind) = 454`.
- **Step 4 — section cuts + design handoff + finalize.** A 1-story wall cuts as a SINGLE-story elevation (route to `SecDiagram`, or `SecDiagram2` with H₂=0); asymmetric cut (1-story front / 2-story back) draws front at its own height, leeward height/parapet from the back wall. Handoff: `buildFloor(2)` on the filtered graph, `buildFloor(1)` with accumulation; a 1-story floor-1 line has no aligned floor-2 partner so it stays UNSTACKED automatically (existing `stackedLineResults`). Also revisit the rev-34 floor-1 `divides` hide so it suppresses only on two-story walls (1-story walls vary along their length and should show divides).
- **Other confirmed details:** accumulation amount = ½·H₂·pw, one face (✅ user). One-story parapets → floor diaphragm; two-story parapets → roof diaphragm (✅). Two-story region assumed to CLOSE into a loop — exact for a freestanding/convex box; an open set falls back to the centroid-normal heuristic — acceptable for v1 (✅). The all-1-story warning is the agreed degenerate handling (✅). rev-34's floor-only display stays valid: it was the UNIFORM two-story special case where the only parapet is at the roof, so nothing connects a parapet to the floor diaphragm; the mixed case legitimately gains floor-level parapet terms.

**Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` all UNCHANGED.

## 4kk. Rev 36 — Mixed-height two-story · Step 2/4: 2nd-floor (roof diaphragm) excludes 1-story walls

Step 2 makes the tag *do* something. On the 2nd-floor view (and the floor-2 design lines), a 1-story wall no longer participates in the roof diaphragm — it collects no line load, casts no overlap-shadow, and takes no point-load reaction. Only the two-story walls carry the roof. The 1st-floor view and 1-story mode are unchanged (floor-1 effects are Step 3). Matches the user's "2ND FLOOR PLAN" schematic (loads + reactions only on the 2-story box).

- **`twoStoryGraph` (new memo).** `if(!twoStory || oneStory.size===0) return graph;` else `{ edges: graph.edges.filter(e=>!oneStory.has(keyOf(e))), nodes: graph.nodes.filter(used) }` where `used` = node ids still referenced by the kept edges. So an untagged building returns the SAME `graph` reference → byte-identical downstream.
- **`twoStoryLoop` (new memo).** `loopInfo(twoStoryGraph.nodes, twoStoryGraph.edges)`. NB: a perimeter+box footprint is TWO rings, so the full-graph `loop` is already `null` (loopInfo wants one cycle covering all nodes) and `buildSecData` uses its centroid-normal fallback; but the filtered two-story graph is just the box = ONE ring → `twoStoryLoop` is non-null → exact exterior normals for the box.
- **Live render.** `const roofView = twoStory && activeFloor===2; secGraph = roofView?twoStoryGraph:graph; secLoop = roofView?twoStoryLoop:loop;` then `secH`/`secV` call `buildSecData(sections.*, secGraph, secLoop, isSup, propsForActive)` (deps swapped graph/loop → secGraph/secLoop). Both are stable references (one of two memoized/state objects), so no extra recompute. Walls still all RENDER off the full `graph` — green 1-story walls are drawn, just load-less on floor 2.
- **Design handoff.** `buildFloor(floor)` gained `fg/fl` locals (`= twoStory&&floor===2 ? twoStoryGraph/twoStoryLoop : graph/loop`) used in its two `buildSecData` calls, the reaction→edge lookup (`fg.edges.find`), the node lookups (`fg.nodes.find`), and the support-extent scan (`fg.edges.forEach`). `runDesignHandoff` deps gained `twoStoryGraph`, `twoStoryLoop`.
- **Why filter the graph instead of zeroing props:** the guarded `buildSecData` runs an `overlapShadow` test that drops a windward wall when another windward wall sits in front of it. A 1-story wall geometrically in FRONT of the box (e.g. the perimeter) would wrongly *shadow* the box's windward wall if it stayed in the graph with zero load. Removing it from the graph excludes it from windward collection, the shadow test, AND `lineReactions` supports in one move — and the guarded engine is never edited.

**Engine guard CLEAN** (all 12 fns identical to the rev-34 baseline). esbuild compile clean; SSR render smoke PASS (32,149 chars). New checked-in **`work/test_step2.cjs`** (6 asserts through the REAL bundled engine on a perimeter-1-story + box-2-story fixture: full graph loads some perimeter wall; FILTERED graph loads no perimeter wall, still loads a box wall, confines reactions to box walls, and yields a base shear that is `>0` but `<` the full-graph base shear). `APP_BUILD = 116` ("Version 1.16").

**Still to do:** Step 3 (1st-floor 454 accumulation — a NEW wind fn that extends the back-wall subdivision pattern to add the back two-story wall's ½·H₂·pw, reusing `lineReactions`; also revisit the rev-34 floor-1 `divides` hide so it suppresses only on two-story walls) · Step 4 (1-story section cut = single-story elevation; asymmetric cut; design-handoff finalize incl. 1-story floor-1 lines staying unstacked).

**Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` all UNCHANGED.

## 4ll. Rev 37 — Mixed-height two-story · Step 3/4: 1st-floor (floor diaphragm) accumulation — "the 454"

The 1st-floor view + floor-1 design now show the mixed building's true floor-diaphragm demand. A windward wall's plf varies along its length, summing the strips connected to the floor diaphragm in its downwind shadow. Worked example (user's schematic): a 1-story perimeter front wall reads `32×5 + 16×13/2 + 22×5 = 374` where nothing two-story stands behind it, and `+ 16×10/2 = 454` over the stretch where the 2-story box does — split by a dashed tributary divide.

- **`buildSecDataF1(section, graph, loop, isSup, propsFor, isOne)` (new module fn, after `buildSecData`).** A focused copy of `buildSecData`: identical windward determination, `overlapShadow`, line-grouping, back-wall `backs` gathering + breakpoint subdivision, `divides`, and reaction aggregation; calls `findLeewardPartner` and `lineReactions` verbatim. Only the per-wall / per-sub-region load rule differs. `isOne(key)` = the wall is tagged 1-story. **Pass it the RAW `propsFor` (mergeWallProps), NOT `propsForActive`** — the fn applies the floor-diaphragm formula itself.
- **Load rule.** `baseOf(key)` = ½·H·pw + (1-story ? par·qWind : ½·H₂·pw). For each windward sub-region: `plf = base + leePar·qLee + acc`, where `leePar` = farthest-downwind back wall's parapet but only counted if THAT back wall `isOne` (a 2-story back wall's parapet is at the roof, not the floor), and `acc` = ½·H₂·pw of the NEAREST 2-story back wall covering the sub-region (one face). `backs[]` now carries `{lo,hi,d, par:(one?bp.par:0), h2:(one?0:½·H₂·pw)}`; the box's lo/hi become breakpoints, so the front wall splits into 374/454.
- **Wiring.** `mixed1 = twoStory && activeFloor===1 && oneStory.size>0`. `secH`/`secV` use `buildSecDataF1(…graph,loop…propsFor,isOneStory)` when `mixed1`, else `buildSecData(…secGraph,secLoop…propsForActive)` (deps add `mixed1,propsFor,isOneStory`). `buildFloor(1)` mirrors it via local `mixedF1`. The rev-34 floor-1 `displayPlf` override and the `divides` hide are both re-gated `…activeFloor===1 && !mixed1`, so the mixed wall shows its real per-region labels + divides, and uniform 2-story (no tags) is byte-identical to rev 36.
- **Self-consistency.** A 2-story windward wall's `base` = ½·H·pw + ½·H₂·pw = `floorDiaphragmPlf` (the rev-34 floor-only value), so the two models agree where they overlap. The box's near face is shadowed-and-dropped from its own windward line by `overlapShadow`; its floor contribution is RECOVERED onto the front wall via `acc` (no double count). The roof half of the box still goes to floor-2 / stacks down separately (Step 2 + existing stacking).

**Engine guard CLEAN** (12/12 identical to the rev-34 baseline). esbuild compile clean; SSR render smoke PASS (32,149); Step-2 regression PASS. New checked-in **`work/test_step3.cjs`** (real `buildSecDataF1` on a 1-story-perimeter 40×30 + 2-story-box x:10–30/y:9–21 fixture, N–S wind): asserts the windward bottom wall's sub-region plfs are `[374,374,454]`, the high−low difference is exactly ½·H₂·pw = 80, the middle third (over the box) carries 454, the box walls are absent from `windLoads` (shadowed → accumulated), and a divide is emitted. `APP_BUILD = 117` ("Version 1.17").

**Still to do — Step 4 (final):** section cuts (a 1-story wall cuts as a SINGLE-story elevation — route to `SecDiagram`, or `SecDiagram2` with H₂=0; asymmetric 1-story-front / 2-story-back draws front at its own height with leeward read from the back wall); design-handoff finalize (confirm 1-story floor-1 lines stay UNSTACKED — they have no aligned floor-2 partner, so `stackedLineResults` already leaves them alone). Then full mixed-height sign-off.

**Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` all UNCHANGED.

## 4mm. Rev 38 — Mixed-height two-story · Step 4/4 (FINAL): section cuts + handoff finalize — FEATURE COMPLETE

Last step. A 1-story wall now cuts as a single-story elevation, and the design stacking was confirmed correct with no change.

- **Section cut.** `WindWindow` gained prop `oneStory` (passed `oneStory={isOneStory(activeWall.key)}` at its single invocation). Inside, `const twoStoryView = twoStory && !oneStory;` now drives BOTH the diagram (`twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2 …/> : <SecDiagram/>`) and the breakdown block (`twoStoryView ? <roof + 2nd-floor split> : <single "Total wall line load">`). So a 1-story cut wall renders the 1-story elevation + total even in 2-story mode; a 2-story cut wall is unchanged. `SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` themselves are untouched — pure routing.
- **Stacking (no code change, by design).** A 1-story wall is excluded from the floor-2 filtered graph (Step 2), so `buildFloor(2)` emits no floor-2 line with its key. In `DesignTab.resultsByLine`, `ln2 = upper.find(L=>L.id===ln.id)` is therefore `undefined` for a 1-story floor-1 line → it uses `lineResults` (unstacked), not `stackedLineResults`. Correct: a 1-story wall carries no roof, so nothing stacks onto it; the box's roof stacks onto the BOX's own 1st-floor lines (which DO have floor-2 partners).
- **Verification.** Engine guard CLEAN (12/12). esbuild compile clean; SSR render smoke PASS (32,149). New **`work/test_step4.cjs`** SSR-renders `WindWindow`: 1-story cut → contains "Total wall line load", excludes "Roof diaphragm line load" + "2nd-floor diaphragm line load"; 2-story cut → contains both split labels; 1-story mode → single total. Steps 2 & 3 regression tests still PASS. `APP_BUILD = 118` ("Version 1.18").

## 4oo. Rev 40 — Mixed-height two-story · sequence-based overall section cut (A/B/C/C-reverse)

The section-cut window is now a true overall-building section, driven by the ordered run of walls the cut crosses. Resolves the two issues the user raised on rev 39 (the section changed between floors; Section C drew like Section A) and renders all four schematic section types.

- **Section type = wall sequence.** `sectionSequence(sAcross, axis, sign, graph, propsFor, isOne)` (module fn after `nearestTwoStoryBehind`) returns every `recv`-orientation wall whose across-wind span includes the cut position `sAcross`, ordered by downwind depth (windward→leeward): `[{key, one, H, H2, par, pw, qWind, qLee, depth}]`. The 1/2-story pattern is the type: `1·2·2·1`=A, `1·1`=B, `1·2·2`=C, `2·2·1`=C-reverse. Always the full graph → floor-independent.
- **Floor independence.** The open-section `useEffect` now computes `seq` from `po.sAcross` on the full graph and anchors `activeWall.key = seq[0].key` (the true windward wall) rather than the floor-filtered `sc.windLoads[0]`. `activeSection.seq` is recomputed from `activeWall.sAcross` (fallback: the active wall's center).
- **`SecDiagramSeq`** (replaced `SecDiagramMix`). Draws N walls front→back at their own story heights; floor diaphragm dashed across all at the 1-story top; roof diaphragm over the contiguous 2-story block (`twoIdx`); windward pressure on the front wall (full height + parapet), leeward on the back; front & back editable through the live `v`/`upd` buffer (front gets an H₂ box when it is 2-story, for C-reverse), interior walls display-only. No per-type branching — the sequence is the input.
- **`WindWindow` routing.** `seq = section.seq||[]`; `hasOne/hasTwo`; `mixedSeq = twoStory && hasOne && hasTwo && seq.length>=2`. `mixedSeq ? <SecDiagramSeq seq floorLL={floorLLmix}> : twoStoryView ? <SecDiagram2> : <SecDiagram>`. `floorLLmix = seqBase + seqLeePar + seqAcc` with `seqBase = ½·H·pw + (front 1-story ? windPar : 0)`, `seqAcc = front 1-story ? ½·H₂·pw of the nearest 2-story in the sequence : ½·H₂·pw of the front wall`, `seqLeePar` only if the back wall is 1-story — matching `buildSecDataF1`. Breakdown shows ½·H·pw + parapets + the poured-forward ½·H₂·pw (478 at H₂=13).

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2`/the guarded engine untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12); compile clean; render smoke PASS. New **`work/test_step5.cjs`** PASSES (A→[1,2,2,1], B→[1,1], C→[1,2,2], C-rev→[2,2,1]; floor-independent; `SecDiagramSeq` draws 2+2 / 1+2 markers; C-reverse front designs a 2-story wall). `test_step4b.cjs` retired (asserted on the removed `SecDiagramMix`). Steps 2/3/4 regressions pass. `APP_BUILD = 120` ("Version 1.20").

## 4pp. Rev 41 — Mixed-height two-story · section cut draws the Level-2 (roof) pressures + value; diaphragms renamed Level 1 / Level 2

Three display-only fixes to `SecDiagramSeq` (the mixed overall-building section cut), driven by the user comparing it to the CAD schematic (SECTION A / SECTION C). The guarded engine and every load value are byte-identical.

- **Block pressures drawn (the missing roof-diaphragm source).** rev 40's `SecDiagramSeq` drew windward pressure only on the sequence FRONT wall and leeward parapet only on the sequence BACK wall; the 2-story block in the middle drew as bare lines — so the pressures that produce the upper diaphragm had no visible source. New draw group: front-most 2-story wall `bw=twoIdx[0]` gets WINDWARD `pw` arrows over its UPPER story (`topY(fw)`→its own floor line; the lower story is shadowed by whatever stands in front) + `qWind` arrows over its parapet; back-most 2-story wall `bl=twoIdx[last]` gets its LEEWARD parapet `qLee` (arrows to the right). Gated `bw!==0` / `bl!==last` so a block end that coincides with the sequence front/back (Section C / C-reverse, already drawn by the front-windward / back-leeward code) isn't drawn twice. Block parapet pressures read `seq[bw].qWind` / `seq[bl].qLee` (the back-block leeward pressure is NOT `W[bl].q`, which is the interior wall's `qWind`). Arrow lengths via a new `aOf(psf)=psf>0?max(psf·aS,6):0`; `maxPsf` (the arrow scale) now spans every wall's `pw/qWind/qLee` so block arrows stay proportional and within the 30px budget.
- **Level-2 (roof) value shown.** `WindWindow` computes `roofLLseq` from the block's front/back `seq` walls: `twoIxSeq = seq indices of !one walls`, `bf=twoIxSeq[0]`, `bb=twoIxSeq[last]`; `roofLLseq = ½·blkH2·blkPw + blkWPar + blkLPar`, where `blkH2/blkPw` come from the front block wall, `blkWPar = front.par·front.qWind`, `blkLPar = back.par·back.qLee` — and where a block end equals the editable sequence front (`bf===0`) / back (`bb===seq.length-1`) the live `v` values (`v.H2/v.pw/v.wH·v.wQ` / `v.lH·v.lQ`) substitute, so Section C / C-reverse edits flow through. Same SHAPE as the uniform-two-story `roofLL = ½·H₂·pw + windPar + leePar`. Passed to `SecDiagramSeq` as a `roofLL` prop, rendered in the upper callout (replacing "→ block's own walls"), and added to the breakdown panel as a "Level 2 diaphragm line load → designs the level-2 (2-story block) walls" section with `½·H₂·pw (block, upper ½)` + `windward + leeward parapet (block)` sub-rows (gated `roofLLseq>0`). Schematic case 10ft/16psf + 6ft·(32+22): `½·10·16 + 6·32 + 6·22 = 404 plf`.
- **Rename → Level 1 / Level 2 (and the naming implication).** Every user-facing "roof diaphragm" → **"Level 2 diaphragm"**, "floor"/"2nd-flr"/"2nd-floor diaphragm" → **"Level 1 diaphragm"**, across `SecDiagramSeq`, `SecDiagram2`, and both `WindWindow` breakdown panels; the "designs Nth-floor shear walls" sublabels → "designs the level-N (upper/lower) shear walls". The mapping is unambiguous because two conventions agree: name-by-the-story-it-designs (roof designs the level-2/upper walls; floor designs the level-1/lower walls) AND name-by-elevation (the lower/first diaphragm = Level 1, the upper/second = Level 2) both give **roof = Level 2, floor = Level 1**. The rename is confined to displayed strings + the comments at the label sites. The `roofLL` / `floorLL` / `roofLLseq` / `floorLLmix` VARIABLE names are intentionally KEPT (a mapping comment was added at their definitions) — renaming identifiers would be pure churn next to the guarded-engine-adjacent UI and buys nothing functional. **No value, engine, reaction, load-path, or design-handoff change** — purely the labels a user reads.
- **Overlap fix.** The rev-40 callout sat at `calloutX=VBW-84=278` while the leeward wall was at `rightX=284`, so the "… diaphragm … plf" text overlapped the wall line (visible in the user's screenshots). Fixed by widening `VBW 362→380`, pulling the wall span left (`rightX 284→250`), and moving the callouts to `calloutX=300` — clear of the wall (250) and its leeward arrows (≤30 → 280).

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` geometry and the guarded wind + shear-wall engines untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); modular compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular render ≡ inlined preview). NEW focused SSR render test (Section A 1·2·2·1, in `work/_rev41_focus.cjs` against an exports-augmented copy): "Level 1 diaphragm" + "Level 2 diaphragm" present, zero legacy "Roof/Floor/2nd-floor diaphragm" strings, Level-2 value `404` rendered, block pressure arrows drawn (26 `dArrM` lines vs the pre-block count), and `calloutX(300) > rightX(250)+arrows(280)`. Steps 2/3/4/5 regressions + engine guard pass. `APP_BUILD = 121` ("Version 1.21").

**Known limitation (RESOLVED in rev 42 — see §4qq):** rev 41 read the block's PLAN props and the interior block walls were display-only. rev 42 makes every wall in the section cut editable (height + pressure), so an interior block wall can now be changed directly and the Level-2 value/arrows follow.

## 4qq. Rev 42 — Mixed-height two-story · interior block walls fully editable (height + pressure)

The floating input branches on `edit.key`: keyed → value `ebuf ?? String(seqVal)`, `onChange` → `setEbuf` + `commit(key,prop,num)`, `onBlur` clears the buffer entry; unkeyed → the existing `v`/`upd` path. Enter/Escape blur (runs the keyed cleanup).
- **Live with no extra wiring.** A keyed edit writes `wallProps[key]`; `propsFor` and thus `activeSection.seq`/`section.seq` recompute every render, and `roofLLseq` (Level-2 value), the floor accumulation `seqAcc` (Level-1), and `propOf(interior)` (the drawing) all already read from `seq`. So a block-wall height/pressure edit flows straight into the values and arrows — identical behavior to a front/back edit, which goes through `v` and also writes `wallProps`.

## 4rr. Rev 43 — Mixed-height two-story · section-cut diaphragms connect to each wall's top + deform on height edit

The user asked to bring two behaviors of the original 1-story `SecDiagram` into the mixed `SecDiagramSeq`: (1) editing a wall's pressure/height updates the Level 1 / Level 2 diaphragm values; (2) the nodes are connected so changing a wall height makes the shape deform. `SecDiagram` (the reference) reads all geometry from the live `v` buffer — `roofYL=wallBot−HL·pxPerFt`, `roofYR=wallBot−HR·pxPerFt` — and draws the wall as a trapezoid whose top edge is the ROOF LINE (a 2-point connector between the windward and leeward tops), with node circles at those tops that reposition live; its line load reads `v` too. Display/UI only — the guarded engine is byte-identical.

- **What was wrong (behaviour 2).** `SecDiagramSeq` drew the floor diaphragm as ONE flat `<line>` at `yF2 = wallBot − max(H)·pxPerFt` and the roof diaphragm as one flat `<line>` at `yRoof = wallBot − max(H+H₂)·pxPerFt`, with each wall an independent vertical. A non-tallest wall's top sat below the flat diaphragm (a gap); editing its height moved only that stub, and the pinned-flat diaphragm made height edits read as inert.
- **Fix.** New per-wall levels `floorY(i)=wallBot−W[i].H·pxPerFt` (a wall's 1st-story top = its Level-1 node) and `roofY(i)=wallBot−(W[i].H+(one?0:H₂))·pxPerFt` (a 2-story wall's full top = its Level-2 node). The Level-1 diaphragm is now a `<polyline>` through `floorY(i)` for every wall + a node `<circle r=2>` at each; the Level-2 diaphragm is a `<polyline>` through `roofY(i)` over the block (`twoIdx`) + nodes. Each wall's drawn top (`topY`) equals its diaphragm node, so they connect; change any H/H₂ and the node moves → the diaphragm slopes/steps → the section deforms as one connected shape (the 1-story sloping roof, generalized to N walls). With uniform heights the polylines are flat == the old look (no regression). The value callouts anchor to the diaphragm's leeward end (`cFloorY=floorY(last)`, `cRoofY=roofY(twoIdx[last])`) so they ride the slope; the parapet-start node moved from the wall top to the parapet TOP (`pty`, smaller `r=1.7`) so it no longer double-draws over a diaphragm node.
- **Behaviour 1 — already live, confirmed.** `WindWindow` computes `floorLLmix`/`roofLLseq` from `section.seq` and `v` in its render body, and `activeSection.seq` is recomputed from `propsFor` (=`wallProps`) every App render. So a block-wall edit (interior `commit`→`wallProps`) or a front/back edit (`v`/`upd`, which also writes `wallProps`) flows into the values: editing a block wall's H₂/pw raises Level 1 (the poured-forward ½·H₂·pw `seqAcc`) AND Level 2 (the block's ½·H₂·pw); parapet edits raise the parapet terms. The leeward wall's HEIGHT changes the SHAPE only (now visibly, via the polyline), not the load value — exactly like the 1-story, where `HR` tilts the roof line but `wallRes` uses the windward `HL`.

`SecDiagram`/`SecDiagram2` and the guarded engines untouched. Engine guard CLEAN (12/12 byte-identical); compile clean; render smoke PASS (modular ≡ inlined preview). rev-41 + rev-42 regressions still 8/8. NEW **`work/_rev43_connect.cjs`** PASSES 10/10: with a Section A cut given DISTINCT heights — the floor diaphragm is a 4-point polyline that slopes to the short leeward wall (connected, deforms); the roof diaphragm is a 2-point polyline that slopes when the two block walls' H₂ differ; ≥6 connection nodes are drawn; a UNIFORM building gives a FLAT floor diaphragm (no regression); and the Level-2 value rises 404→484 when the block H₂ goes 10→20 and →474 when the block pw goes 16→30 (so height AND pressure edits update the values). `APP_BUILD = 123` ("Version 1.23").

**Deploy:** replace `src/plan-sketcher-suite.jsx` ONLY — `calcCore.js`, `main.jsx`, `index.html`, `package.json`, `vite.config.js` all UNCHANGED.

## 4ss. Rev 44 — Mixed-height two-story · leeward-most wall height editable (geometry-only) + default wall height 10ft

Two user-requested fixes.

- **Leeward-most wall height editable.** The user observed that the 1-story `SecDiagram` lets you edit the leeward wall's height (`v.leeH` → the `leeH` box → `setVals("lee",{H})`) for correct geometry even though that wall carries no load, and asked for the same on the mixed cut's LAST wall in the wind direction. `SecDiagramSeq`'s back-box group previously gated the WHOLE group on `w.par>0` and exposed only the leeward parapet (`qLee`) + parapet height — the wall's HEIGHT was fixed. It now ALWAYS renders an `H` box (`field="leeH" prop="leeH"`) and, when the back wall is 2-story (Section C, `!w.one`), an `H₂` box (`field="leeH2" prop="leeH2"`); the parapet pressure/height boxes remain gated on `par>0`. `upd` already maps `leeH`→`setVals("lee",{H})` and `leeH2`→`setVals("lee",{H2})`, and `propOf(last)` already reads `v.leeH`/`v.leeH2`, and the open-section seed populates them from the leeward partner — so editing flows into the rev-43 connected diaphragm polyline and the back wall redraws/deforms (its top node moves). Geometry-only: it routes through `upd`/`"lee"` (not the interior `commit` path) and does NOT change the Level-1/Level-2 load values, exactly like the 1-story where `wallRes` uses the windward `HL` and `HR` only sets the roof slope.
- **Default wall height 10ft.** `DEF_SECTION.H: 13 → 10` (parapet already 5; `H₂` is null → equals H, so a new wall is H=10, H₂=10, par=5). VALUE-only change — no field renamed/added/removed, so the load-state schema tripwire (which locks field NAMES; verified historically to trip on an `H2`→`h2` rename) is unaffected. Re-run `test_schema.cjs` in the full harness to confirm; if it ALSO snapshots default values, update `schema.expected.json` (the change is intentional). `mergeWallProps` only fills MISSING keys, so existing saved `.wps` files keep their stored heights — this affects NEW walls only.
